   CHAPTER 1	CHA aPTER 1
   VAJRADHATU MAHA MANDALA VIDHI VISTARA MANDALA I.1	Va aJRa aDHATU MAHA a MANDALA  VIDHI  VI STARA MANDALAH I.1
   [evaṃ mayā śru]tamekasmin samaye bhagavān	[evam mayA Sru]tam ekasmin samaye BagavAn
   sarvatathāgata vajrādhiṣṭhānasamayajñānavividhaviśeṣasamanvāgataḥ,	sarva taTAgata  vajra aDizWAna samaya jQAna viviDa viSeza samanvAgataH,
   sarvatathāgataratnamukuṭatraidhātukadharmarājyābhiṣekaprāptaḥ,	sarva taTAgata ratna mukuwa trEDAtuka Darma rAjya aBizeka prAptaH,
   sarvatathāgatasarvajñānamahāyogīśvaraḥ,	sarva taTAgata sarva jQAna mahA yogi ISvaraH,
   sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāsamatādhigataviśvakāryakaraṇatāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvāśāparipūrakaḥ,	sarva taTAgata sarvamudrA samatA aDigata viSva kArya karaNa tA SezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva ASAparipUrakaH,
   mahākṛpo vairocanaḥ śāśvatastryadhvasamayavyavasthitaḥ	mahAkRpaH vErocanaH SASvataH tri aDva samaya vyavasTitaH
   sarvakāyavākcittavajrastathāgataḥ, sarvatathāgatādhyuṣitapraśastastavite	sarva kAya vAc citta vajraH taTAgataH, sarva taTAgata aDyuzita praSasta stavite
   mahāmaṇiratnapratyupte	mahA maNi ratna pratyupte
   vicitravarṇaghaṇṭāvasaktamārutoddhatapaṭṭasrakcāmarahārārdhahāracandropaśobhite	vicitra varNa GaNwA avasakta mAruta udData pawwa sraj ca amara hAra arDa hAra candra upaSoBite
   akaniṣṭhadevarājasya bhavane vijahāra / navanavatibhirbodhisattvakoṭibhiḥ	akanizWa deva rAjasya Bavane vijahAra / navanavatiBiH boDisattva kowiBiH
   sārdhaṃ, tadyathā vajrapāṇinā ca bodhisattvena, avalokiteśvareṇa ca	sArDaM, tat yaTA vajrapANinA ca boDisattvena, avalokita ISvareNa ca
   bodhisattvena, ākāśagarbheṇa ca, vajramuṣṭinā ca, mañjuśriyā ca,	boDisattvena, AkASa garBeNa ca, vajramuzwinA ca, maQju SriyA ca,
   sahacittotpādadharmacakrapravartinā ca, gaganagañjena ca	saha citta utpAda Darma cakra pravartinA ca, gagana gaQjena ca
   sarvamārabalapramardinā ca,	sarvam Ara bala pramardinA ca,
   evaṃpramukhairnavanavatibhirbodhisattvakoṭibhiḥ;	evaMpramuKEH navanavatiBiH boDisattva kowiBiH;
   gaṅgānadīvālukāsamākhyātaiśca tathāgataiḥ, tadyathāpi nāma tilabimbamiva	gaFgA nadI vAlukA samAKyAtEH ca taTAgatEH, tat yaTA api nAma tila bimbam iva
   paripūrṇaṃ jambūdvīpe saṃdṛśyate / taiścāprameyaistathāgatairekaikasmācca	paripUrNam jambUdvIpe saMdRSyate / tEH ca aprameyEH taTAgatEH ekEkasmAt ca
   tathāgatakāyādaprameyāsaṃkhyeyāni buddhakṣetrāṇi saṃdṛśyante, teṣu ca	taTAgata kAyAt aprameya asaMKyeyAni budDa kzetrANi saMdRSyante, tezu ca
   buddhakṣetreṣu imameva dharmanayaṃ deśayanti sma /	budDa kzetrezu imam eva Darmanayam deSayanti sma /
   atha bhagavān mahāvairocanaḥ sarvākāśadhātusadāvasthitakāyavākcittavajraḥ	aTa BagavAn mahA vErocanaH sarva AkASa DAtu sada avasTita kAya vAc citta vajraH
   sarvatathāgatasamavasaraṇatayā sarvavajradhātvavabodhanajñānasattvaḥ	sarva taTAgata samavasaraNa tayA sarva vajra DAtu avaboDana jQAna sattvaH
   sarvākāśadhātuparamāṇurajo vajrādhiṣṭhānasambhavajñānagarbhaḥ	sarva AkASa DAtu paramANu rajaH vajra aDizWAna samBava jQAna garBaH
   sarvatathāgatānantatayā mahavajrajñānābhiṣekaratnaḥ	sarva taTAgata ananta tayA maha vajra jQAna aBizeka ratnaH
   sarvākāśaspharaṇatathatājñānābhisambodhyabhisambodhibhūtaḥ	sarva AkASa sParaNa taTatA jQAna aBisamboDi aBisamboDi BUtaH
   sarvatathāgatātmabhāvaśuddhitayāsvabhāvaśuddhasarvadharmaḥ	sarva taTAgata Atma BAva SudDi tayA svaBAva SudDa sarva DarmaH
   sarvākāśacaryāgryaḥ sarvatathāgatāmoghājñākāritayā	sarva AkASa caryA agryaH sarva taTAgatA amoGa AjQA kAri tayA
   sarvāsamānuttaraviśvakarmā / sarvatathāgatamahābodhidṛḍhasattvaḥ	sarva asamA anuttara viSvakarmA / sarva taTAgata mahA boDi dRXa sattvaH
   sarvatathāgatakarṣaṇasamayaḥ sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇajñāneśvaraḥ	sarva taTAgata karzaNa samayaH sarva taTAgata anurAgaNa jQAna ISvaraH
   sarvatathāgatasādhukāraḥ sarvatathāgatamahābhiṣekaratnaḥ	sarva taTAgata sADukAraH sarva taTAgata mahA aBizeka ratnaH
   sarvatathāgatasūryaprabhāmaṇḍalaḥ sarvatathāgatacintārājamaṇiratnaketuḥ	sarva taTAgata sUrya praBA maNxalaH sarva taTAgata cintA rAja maNi ratna ketuH
   sarvatathāgatamahāhāsaḥ sarvatathāgatamahāśuddhadharmaḥ	sarva taTAgata mahA hAsaH sarva taTAgata mahA SudDa DarmaH
   sarvatathāgataprajñājñānaḥ sarvatathāgatacakraḥ	sarva taTAgata prajQA jQAnaH sarva taTAgata cakraH
   sarvatathāgatamahāvīryasudṛḍhakavacaḥ	sarva taTAgata mahA vIrya su dRXa kavacaH
   sarvatathāgatarakṣaparipālanavajrayakṣaḥ	sarva taTAgata rakza paripAlana vajrayakzaH
   sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajrabandhamudrājñānaḥ /	sarva taTAgata kAya vAc citta vajra banDa mudrA jQAnaH /
   Eulogy of Samantabhadra the mahabodhistattva	EulogI of SamantaBadra Te maha boDiH tattva
   samantabhadraḥ svamoghaḥ māraḥ prāmodyanāyakaḥ /	samantaBadraH su amoGaH mAraH prAmodya nAyakaH /
   khagarbhaḥ su[mahāte]jā ratnaketurmahāsmitaḥ // 1 //	KagarBaH su [mahAte]jAH ratnaketuH mahAsmitaH // 1 //
   avalokitamaheśaś ca mañjuśrīḥ sarvamaṇḍalaḥ /	avalokita maheSaH ca maQjuSrIH sarva maNxalaH /
   avāco viśvakarmā ca vīryaścaṇḍo [dṛḍhagrahaḥ] // 2 //	avAcaH viSvakarmA ca vIryaH caNxaH [dRXa grahaH] // 2 //
   vajro 'ṅ kuśaḥ śarastuṣṭiḥ ratnaḥ sūryo dhvajaḥ smitaḥ /	vajraH aF kuSaH SaraH tuzwiH ratnaH sUryaH DvajaH smitaH /
   padmaḥ kośaḥ sucakro vāk karma varma ravayo grahaḥ // 3 //	padmaH koSaH su cakraH vAc karma varma ravayaH grahaH // 3 //
   anādinidha[naḥ śānto rudraḥ krodho mahā]kṣamaḥ /	anAdiniDa[naH SAntaH rudraH kroDaH mahA] kzamaH /
   yakṣaḥ surākṣaso dhīraḥ sauriḥ saurirmahāvibhuḥ // 4 //	yakzaH su rAkzasaH DIraH sOriH sOriH mahA viBuH // 4 //
   umāpatiḥ prajānātho viṣṇurjiṣṇurmahāmuniḥ /	umApatiH prajA nATaH vizNuH jizNuH mahA muniH /
   lokapālo nabho bhūmi[striloka]stu tridhātukaḥ // 5 //	lokapAlaH naBaH BUmi[H triloka]H tu tri DAtukaH // 5 //
   mahābhūtaḥ susattvārthaḥ sarvaḥ śarvaḥ pitāmahaḥ /	mahABUtaH su sattva arTaH sarvaH SarvaH pitAmahaH /
   saṃsāro nirvṛtiḥ śaśvat samyagvṛttirmahāmahaḥ // 6 //	saMsAraH nirvRtiH SaSvat samyak vRttiH mahAmahaH // 6 //
   buddhaḥ śuddho mahāyānastribhavaḥ śāśvato hisaḥ /	budDaH SudDaH mahAyAnaH tri BavaH SASvataH hisaH /
   trilokavijayī śambhuḥ śambhunāthaḥ pradāmakaḥ // 7 // //	triloka vijayI SamBuH SamBunATaH pradAmakaH // 7 // //
   vajranāthaḥ subhūmyagryo jñānaḥ pāramitānayaḥ /	vajra nATaH su BUmi agryaH jQAnaH pAramitA anayaH /
   vimokṣo bodhisattvaśca caryaḥ sarvatathāgataḥ // 8 //	vimokzaH boDisattvaH ca caryaH sarva taTAgataH // 8 //
   buddhārtho buddhahṛdayaḥ sarvabodhiranuttaraḥ /	budDa arTaH budDa hRdayaH sarva boDiH anuttaraH /
   vairocano jino nāthaḥ svayaṃbhūrdhāraṇī smṛtiḥ // 9 //	vErocanaH jinaH nATaH svayaMBUH DAraNI smRtiH // 9 //
   mahāsattvo mahāmudraḥ samādhirbuddhakarmakṛt /	mahAsattvaH mahAmudraH samADiH budDa karma kRt /
   sarvabuddhātmako bhūtaḥ sattvo nityārthabodhakaḥ // 10 //	sarva budDa AtmakaH BUtaH sattvaH nitya arTa boDakaH // 10 //
   mahāsthāṇurmahākālo mahārāgo mahāsukhaḥ /	mahA sTANuH mahAkAlaH mahA rAgaH mahAsuKaH /
   mahāpāpo mahāgryāgryaḥ sarvāgryo bhuvaneśvaraḥ // 11 //	mahA pApaH mahA agrya agryaH sarva agryaH BuvaneSvaraH // 11 //
   bhagavān mahābodhicittaḥ samantabhadro mahābodhisattvaḥ	BagavAn mahA boDi cittaH samantaBadraH mahA boDisattvaH
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayeṣu vijahāra / atha sarvatathāgatairidaṃ buddhakṣetraṃ	sarva taTAgata hRdayezu vijahAra / aTa sarva taTAgatEH idam budDa kzetram
   tadyathā tilabimbamiva paripūrṇama //	tat yaTA tila bimbam iva paripUrNama //
   atha khalu sarvatathāgatā mahāsamājamāpadya, yena	aTa Kalu sarva taTAgatAH mahA samAjam Apadya, yena
   sarvārthasiddhirbodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ bodhimaṇḍaniṣaṇṇastenopajagmuḥ /	sarva arTa sidDiH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH boDimaNxa nizaNNaH tena upajagmuH /
   upetya bodhisattvasya sāṃbhogikaiḥ kāyairdarśanandatvaivamāhuḥ  "kathaṃ	upetya boDisattvasya sa aMBogikEH kAyEH darSanandatvA evam AhuH "kaTam
   kulaputrānuttarāṃ samyaksambodhim abhisaṃbhotsyase, yastvaṃ	kula putrAn uttarAm samyaksamboDim aBisaMBotsyase, yaH tvam
   sarvatathāgatatattvānabhijñatayā sarvaduḥkarāṇyutsahasī ?"ti /	sarva taTAgata tattva anaBijQa tayA sarva duHkarANi utsahasI ?"ti /
   atha sarvārthasiddhirbodhisattvo	aTa sarva arTa sidDiH boDisattvaH 
   mahāsatvassarvatathāgatacoditaḥsamānastata āsphānasamādhito vyutthāya,	mahA satva ssarva taTAgata coditaH samAnaH tatas AsPAna samADitaH vyutTAya,
   sarvatathāgatān praṇipatyāhū yaivamāha  "bhagavantastathāgatā ājñāpayata	sarva taTAgatAn praNipatya AhU yA evam Aha "BagavantaH taTAgatAH AjQApayata
   kathaṃ pratipadyāmi kīdṛśaṃ tat tattvam" iti / evamukte sarvatathāgatāstaṃ	kaTam pratipadyAmi kIdRSam tat tattvam" iti / evam ukte sarva taTAgatAH tam
   bodhisattvamekakaṇṭhenaivamāhuḥ  "pratipadyasva kulaputra	boDisattvam eka kaNWena evam AhuH "pratipadyasva kula putra
   svacittapratyavekṣaṇasamādhānena prakṛtisiddhena rucijaptena mantreṇa" iti	sva citta pratyavekzaNa samADAnena prakRti sidDena ruci japtena mantreNa" iti
   oṃ cittaprativedhaṃ karomi /	om citta prativeDam karomi /
   atha bodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatānevamāha  "ājñātaṃ me	aTa boDisattvaH sarva taTAgatAn evam Aha "a ajQAtam me
   bhagavantastathāgatāḥ svahṛdi candramaṇḍalākāraṃ paśyāmi" /	BagavantaH taTAgatAH sva hRdi candra maNxala AkAram paSyAmi" /
   sarvatathāgatāḥ procuḥ  "prakṛtiprabhāsvaramidaṃ kulaputra cittaṃ,	sarva taTAgatAH procuH "prakRti praBAsvaram idam kula putra cittaM,
   tadyathā parikarṣyate tat tathaiva bhavati / tadyathāpi nāma śvetavastre	tat yaTA parikarzyate tat taTA eva Bavati / tat yaTA api nAma Sveta vastre
   rāgarañjanam" iti /	rAga raQjanam" iti /
   atha sarvatathāgatāḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaracittajñānasya sphītīkaraṇahetoḥ	aTa sarva taTAgatAH prakRti praBA svara citta jQAnasya sPItIkaraNa hetoH
   punarapi tasmai bodhisattvāya oṃ bodhicittamutpādayāmi ityanena	punar api tasmE boDisattvAya om boDi cittam utpAdayAmi iti anena
   prakṛtisiddhena mantreṇa bodhicittamutpāditavantaḥ /	prakRti sidDena mantreNa boDi cittam utpAditavantaH /
   atha bodhisattvaḥ punarapi sarvatathāgatājñayā bodhicittamutpādyaivamāha 	aTa boDisattvaH punar api sarva taTAgata AjQayA boDi cittam utpAdya evam Aha 
   "yat taccandramaṇḍalākāraṃ taccandramaṇḍalameva paśyāmi" / sarvatathāgatā	"yat tad candra maNxala AkAram tat candra maNxalam eva paSyAmi" / sarva taTAgatA
   āhuḥ  "sarvatathāgatahṛdayante samantabhadraścittotpādaḥ sāmīcībhūtaḥ,	AhuH "sarva taTAgata hRdayante samantaBadraH citta utpAdaH sAmIcIBUtaH,
   tatsādhu pratipadyatām, sarvatathāgatasamantabhadracittotpādasya	tat sADu pratipadyatAm, sarva taTAgata samantaBadra citta utpAdasya
   dṛḍhīkaraṇahetoḥ svahṛdi candramaṇḍale vajrabimbaṃ cintayānena mantreṇa oṃ	dRXIkaraNa hetoH sva hRdi candra maNxale vajra bimbam cintayA anena mantreNa om
   tiṣṭha vajra /	tizWa vajra /
   bodhisattva āha  "paśyāmi bhagavantastathāgatāścandramaṇḍale vajram" /	boDisattvaH Aha "paSyAmi BagavantaH taTAgatAH candra maNxale vajram" /
   sarvatathāgatā āhuḥ  "dṛḍhīkurvidaṃ	sarva taTAgatAH AhuH "dRXIkurvidam
   sarvatathāgatasamantabhadracittavajramanena mantreṇa oṃ vajrātmako 'ham //	sarva taTAgata samantaBadra cittava jram anena mantreNa om vajra AtmakaH aham //
   atha yāvantaḥ sarvākāśadhātusamavasaraṇāḥ	aTa yAvantaH sarva AkASa DAtu samavasaraNAH
   sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajradhātavaḥ, te sarve	sarva taTAgatakAya vAc citta vajra DAtavaH, te sarve
   sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena tasmin sattvavajre praviṣṭāḥ / tataḥ	sarva taTAgata aDizWAnena tasmin sattva vajre pravizwAH / tatas 
   sarvatathāgataiḥ sa bhagavān sarvārthasiddhirmahābodhisattvo	sarva taTAgatEH sa BagavAn sarva arTa sidDiH mahA boDisattvaH 
   vajradhāturvajradhāturiti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /	vajraDAtuH vajraDAtuH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH /
   atha vajradhāturmahābodhisattvastān sarvatathāgatānevamāha "paśyāmi	aTa vajraDAtuH mahA boDisattvaH tAn sarva taTAgatAn evam Aha "paSyAmi
   bhagavantastathāgatāḥ sarvatathāgatakāyamātmānam" / sarvatathāgatāḥ	BagavantaH taTAgatAH sarva taTAgata kAyam AtmAnam" / sarva taTAgatAH
   prāhuḥ  "tena hi mahāsattva sattvavajraṃ sarvākāravaropetaṃ	prAhuH "tena hi mahA sattva sattva vajram sarva AkAra vara upetam
   buddhabimbamātmānaṃ bhāvayānena prakṛtisiddhena mantreṇa rucitaḥ parijapya	budDa bimbam AtmAnam BAva yAnena prakRti sidDena mantreNa rucitaH parijapya
   oṃ yathā sarvatathāgatāstathāham" //	om yaTA sarva taTAgatAH taTA aham" //
   athaivamukte vajradhāturmahābodhisattvastathāgatamātmānamabhisambudhya,	aTa evam ukte vajraDAtuH mahA boDisattvaH taTAgatam AtmAnam aBisambuDya,
   tān sarvatathāgatān praṇipatyāhū yaivamāha "adhitiṣṭhata māṃ	tAn sarva taTAgatAn praNipatya AhU yA evam Aha "aDitizWata mAm
   bhagavantastathāgatā imāmabhisaṃbodhiṃ dṛḍhīkuruta ceti" / athaivamukte	BagavantaH taTAgatAH imAm aBisaMboDim dRXIkuruta ceti" / aTa evam ukte
   sarvatathāgatā vajradhātostathāgatasya tasmin sattvavajre praviṣṭā iti //	sarva taTAgatAH vajraDAtoH taTAgatasya tasmin sattva vajre pravizwAH iti //
   atha bhagavān vajradhātustathāgatastasmin eva kṣaṇe	aTa BagavAn vajraDAtuH taTAgataH tasmin eva kzaNe
   sarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhisaṃbuddha	sarva taTAgata samatA jQAna aBisaMbudDa
   sarvatathāgatavajrasamatājñānamudrāguhyasamayapraviṣṭaḥ	sarva taTAgata vajra samatA jQAna mudrA guhya samaya pravizwaH
   sarvatathāgatadharmasamatājñānādhigamasvabhāvaśuddhaḥ	sarva taTAgata Darma samatA jQAna aDigama svaBAva SudDaH
   sarvatathāgatasarvasamatāprakṛtiprabhāsvarajñānākarabhūtastathāgato 'rhān	sarva taTAgata sarva sama tA prakRti praBA svara jQAna Akara BUtaH taTAgataH arhAn
   samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ saṃvṛtta iti //	samyaksaMbudDaH saMvRttaH iti //
   atha sarvatathāgatāḥ punarapi tataḥ sarvatathāgatasattvavajrān	aTa sarva taTAgatAH punar api tatas sarva taTAgata sattva vajrAn
   niḥsṛtyākāśagarbhamahāmaṇiratnābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicyāvalokiteśvaradharmajñānamutpādya	niHsRtya AkASa garBa mahA maNi ratna aBizekeNa aBizicya avalokita ISvara Darma jQAnam utpAdya
   sarvatathāgataviśvakarmatāyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yena sumerugirimūrdhā yena ca	sarva taTAgata viSva karma tAyAm pratizWApya yena sumeru giri mUrDA yena ca
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārastenopasaṃkrāntāḥ, upasaṃkramya	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa agAraH tena upasaMkrAntAH, upasaMkramya
   vajradhātuntathāgataṃ sarvatathāgatatve 'dhiṣṭhya, sarvatathāgatasiṃhāsane	vajraDAtun taTA gatam sarva taTAgata tve aDizWya, sarva taTAgata siMhAsane
   sarvatomukhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayāmāsuriti //	sarvatomuKam pratizWApayAmAsuH iti //
   Emanation of the 37 deities from samadhi	Emanation of Te 37 deitieH from samaDi
   atha khalu akṣobhyastathāgato ratnasaṃbhavaśca tathāgato lokeśvararājaśca	aTa Kalu akzoByaH taTAgataH ratna saMBavaH ca taTAgataH loka ISvara rAjaH ca
   tathāgato amoghasiddhiśca tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatatvaṃ	taTAgataH amoGa sidDiH ca taTAgataH sarva taTAgata tvam
   svayamātmanyadhiṣṭhāya, bhagavataḥ śākyamunestathāgatasya	svayam Atmani aDizWAya, BagavataH SAkya muneH taTAgatasya
   sarvasamatāsuprativedhatvāt sarvadiksamatāmabhyālambya, catasṛṣu dikṣu	sarva sama tAsu prativeDa tvAt sarva diS samatAm aByAlambya, catasRzu dikzu
   niṣaṇṇāḥ //	nizaNNAH //
   I.1.6 Vajrasattva	I.1.6 Vajra sattva
   atha bhagavān vairocanastathāgataḥ acirābhisaṃbuddhaḥ	aTa BagavAn vErocanaH taTAgataH acira aBisaMbudDaH
   sarvatathāgatasamantabhadrahṛdayasarvatathāgatākāśasaṃbhavamahāmaṇiratnābhiṣekābhiṣiktaḥ	sarva taTAgata samantaBadra hRdaya sarva taTAgata AkASa saMBava mahA maNi ratna aBizeka aBiziktaH
   sarvatathāgatāvalokiteśvaradharmajñānaparamapāramitāprāptaḥ	sarva taTAgata avalokita ISvara Darma jQAna parama pAramitA prAptaH
   sarvatathāgataviśvakarmatāmoghāpratihataśāsanaḥ paripūrṇakāryaḥ	sarva taTAgata viSva karma tA moGa apratihata SAsanaH paripUrNa kAryaH
   paripūrṇamanorathaḥ sarvatathāgatatvaṃ svayamātmanyadhiṣṭhāya,	paripUrNa manoraTaH sarva taTAgata tvam svayam Atmani aDizWAya,
   sarvatathāgatasamantabhadramahābodhisattvasamayasambhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ	sarva taTAgata samantaBadra mahA boDisattva samaya samBava sattva aDizWAna vajram
   nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayaṃ nāma	nAma samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAgata mahA yAna aBisamayam nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayāna niścacāra vajrasattva //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAna niScacAra vajra sattvaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavāṃ	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarvaTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   samantabhadraścandramaṇḍalāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, sarvasattvānāṃ	samantaBadraH candra maNxalAni BUtvA viniHsRtya, sarva sattvAnAm
   mahābodhicittāni saṃśodhya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ sarvapārśveṣvavasthitāḥ /	mahA boDi cittAni saMSoDya, sarva taTAgatAnAm sarva pArSvezu avasTitAH /
   atha tebhyaścandramaṇḍalebhyaḥ sarvatathāgatajñānavajrāṇi viniḥsṛtya,	aTa teByaH candra maNxaleByaH sarva taTAgata jQAna vajrANi viniHsRtya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya hṛdaye praviṣṭāni /	BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya hRdaye pravizwAni /
   samantabhadratvācca sudṛḍhatvācca vajrasattvasamādheḥ	samantaBadra tvAt ca su dRXa tvAt ca vajra sattva samADeH
   sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena caikadhanaḥ sakalākāśadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo	sarva taTAgata aDizWAnena ca eka DanaH sakala AkASa DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH 
   raśmimālo pañcamūrdhā sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajramayovajravigrahaḥ	raSmimAlaH paQcamUrDA sarva taTAgatakAya vAc citta vajra mayaH vajra vigrahaH
   prādurbhūya, sarvathāgatahṛdayān niṣkramya pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato	prAdurBUya, sarvaTAgata hRdayAt nizkramya pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   vajrād vajrākārā raśmayo vicitravarṇarūpāḥ sarvalokadhātvābhāsanaspharaṇā	vajrAt vajra AkArAH raSmayaH vicitra varNa rUpAH sarva loka DAtu ABAsana sParaNA
   viniścaritāḥ / tebhyaśca vajraraśmimukhebhyaḥ	viniScaritAH / teByaH ca vajra raSmi muKeByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   sakaladharmadhātusamavasaraṇeṣu sarvākāśadhātuparyavasāneṣu	sakala Darma DAtu samavasaraNezu sarva AkASa DAtu paryavasAnezu
   sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudreṣu	sarva loka DAtu prasara meGa samudrezu
   sarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhijñāsvabhisaṃbodhāt,	sarva taTAgata samatA jQAna aBijQAsu aBisaMboDAt,
   sarvatathāgatamahābodhicittotpādanasamantabhadravividhacaryāniṣpādanasarva 	sarva taTAgata mahA boDi citta utpAdana samantaBadra viviDa caryA nizpAdana sarva 
   tathāgatakulārāgaṇamahābodhimaṇḍopasaṃkramaṇasarvamāradharṣaṇasarva 	taTAgata kulArA gaNa mahA boDi maNxa upasaMkramaNa sarva mAra DarzaNa sarva 
   tathāgatasamatāmahābodhyabhisaṃbudhyanadharmacakrapravartanaṃ yāvad	taTAgata samatA mahA boDyaBisaMbuDyana Darma cakra pravartanam yAvat 
   aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvahitasukhasarvatathāgatajñānābhijñottamasiddhiniṣpādanādīni	aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu paritrANa sarva hita suKa sarva taTAgata jQAna aBijQa uttama sidDi nizpAdana AdIni
   sarvatathāgatavikurvitāni sandarśya, samantabhadratvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ	sarva taTAgata vikurvitAni sandarSya, samantaBadra tvAt vajra sattva samADeH
   sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ samantabhadramahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya,	su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH samantaBadra mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho samantabhadro 'haṃ dṛḍhasattvaḥ svayaṃbhuvāṃ /	aho samantaBadraH aham dRXa sattvaH svayaMBuvAm /
   yad dṛḍhatvādakāyo 'pi sattvakāyatvamāgataḥ //	yat dRXa tvAt akAyaH api sattva kAya tvam AgataH //
   atha samantabhadramahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa samantaBadra mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa //	sarva taTAgatAnAm puratas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA AjQAm mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatajñānasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarvataTAgata jQAna samayavajram nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgataśīlasamādhiprajñāvimuktivimuktijñānadarśanadharmacakrapravartanasattvārthamahopāyabalavīryamahājñānasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvādhipatyasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārtha	sarva taTAgata SIla samADi prajQA vimukti vimukti jQAna darSana Darma cakra pravartana sattva arTa mahA upAya bala vIrya mahA jQAna samayam aSeza anavaS
   yāvat	yAvat 
   sarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhijñānuttaramahāyānābhisamayottamasiddhyavāptiphalahetostatsarvatathāgatasiddhivajraṃ	sarva taTAgata samatA jQAna aBijQA anuttara mahA yAna aBisamaya uttama sidDi avApti Pala hetoH tat sarva taTAgata sidDi vajram
   tasmai samantabhadrāya mahābodhisattvāya sarvatathāgatacakravartitve	tasmE samantaBadrAya mahA boDisattvAya sarva taTAgata cakravarti tve
   sarvabuddhakāyaratnamukuṭapaṭṭābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicya pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt /	sarva budDa kAya ratna mukuwa pawwa aBizekeNa aBizicya pANiByAm anuprAdAt /
   tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajrapāṇirvajrapāṇiriti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ	tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajrapANiH vajrapANiH iti vajra nAmA aBizekeNa aBiziktaH
   atha vajrapāṇirbodhisattvo mahāsattvo vāmavajragarvollālanatayā tadavajraṃ	aTa vajrapANiH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH vAma vajra garva ullAlana tayA tat avajram
   svahṛdyutkarṣaṇayogena dhārayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sva hRdi utkarzaNa yogena DArayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ siddhivajramanuttaraṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm sidDi vajram anuttaram /
   ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ vajraṃ vajre pratiṣṭhitam // iti //	aham mama kare dattam vajram vajre pratizWitam // iti //
   I.1.7 Vajraraja	I.1.7 Vajraraja
   atha bhagavān	aTa BagavAn
   punarapyamogharājamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma	punar api amoGa rAja mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava sattva aDizWAnavajram nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyadaṃ sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇasamayannāma	samADim samApad yadam sarva taTAgata AkarzaNa samayat nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrarāja //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra rAja //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajrapāṇi sarvatathāgatamahāṅkuśāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato	vajrapANi sarva taTAgata mahA aFkuSAni BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrāṅku śamahāvigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH vajra aFku SamahA vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajrāṅku śamahāvigrahāt	BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra aFku SamahA vigrahAt 
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   sarvatathāgatakarṣaṇādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	sarva taTAgata karzaNa AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   svamogharājatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ	su a moGa rAja tvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   amogharājamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	amoGa rAja mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyamogharājāhaṃ vajrasaṃbhavamaṅku śaḥ /	aho hi amoGa rAjA aham vajra saMBavam aFku Sas /
   yatsarvavyāpino buddhāḥ samākṛṣyanti siddhayaḥ // iti //	yat sarva vyApinaH budDAH samAkRzyanti sidDayaH // iti //
   atha so 'mogharājamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa saH amoGa rAja mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm dakziNa candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa //	mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇasamayavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata AkarzaNa samaya vajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvākarṣaṇasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata AkarzaNa samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva AkarzaNa sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgatasamājādhiṣṭhānottamasiddhyarthaṃ tadvajrāṅkuśaṃ tasmai	yAvat sarva taTAgata samAja aDizWAna uttama sidDi arTam tat vajrAFkuSam tasmE
   amogharājāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	amoGa rAjAya mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajrākarṣo vajrākarṣa iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatEH vajra AkarzaH vajra AkarzaH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajrākarṣo bodhisattvastena vajrāṅkuśena	aTa vajra AkarzaH boDisattvaH tena vajra aFkuSena
   sarvatathāgatānākarṣayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sarva taTAgatAn Akarzayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ vajrajñānamanuttaraṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm vajra jQAnam anuttaram /
   yatsarvabuddhārthasiddhyartha samākarṣaṇamuttamama // iti //	yat sarva budDa arTa sidDi arTa samAkarzaNam uttamamaH // iti //
   I.1.8 Vajraraga	I.1.8 Vajra raga
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   māramahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ	mAra mahAboDisattva samaya saMBava sattva aDizWAnavajram nAma samADim
   samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇasamayannāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samApadya idam sarva taTAgata anurAgaNa samayat nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrarāga //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra rAga //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatakusumāyudhāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata kusuma AyuDAni BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano mahāvajravāṇavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH mahA vajravANa vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato	pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   vajravāṇavigrahātsarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā	vajravANa vigrahAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	viniHsRtya, sarva taTAgata anurAgaNa AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   sumāraṇatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghano	sumAraNa tvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH 
   māramahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	mAra mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho svabhāvaśuddho 'hamanurāgaḥ svayaṃbhuvāṃ /	aho svaBAva SudDaH aham anurAgaH svayaMBuvAm /
   yacchuddhyarthaṃ viraktānāṃ rāgeṇa vinayanti hi //	yat SudDi arTam viraktAnAm rAgeNa vinayanti hi //
   atha sa māramahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya	aTa sa mAra mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa	sarva taTAgatAnAm vAma candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma samādhiṃ	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata anurAgaNa aDizWAna vajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadya,	samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatamāraṇavajrasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣatvadhātvanurāgaṇarsāsukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata mAraNa vajra samayam aSeza anavaSeza tva DAtu anurAgaNarsA suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgatamārakarmottamasiddhyavāptiphalahetostadvajravāṇaṃ	yAvat sarva taTAgata mAra karma uttama sidDi avApti Pala hetoH tat vajravANam
   tasmai mārāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	tasmE mArAya mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajradhanurvajradhanuriti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatEH vajraDanuH vajraDanuH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajradhanurbodhisattvo mahāsattvastena vajravāṇena sarvatathāgatān	aTa vajra DanuH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tena vajravANena sarva taTAgatAn
   mārayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	mArayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idantatsarvabuddhānāṃ rāgajñānamanāvilaṃ /	idantat sarva budDAnAm rAga jQAnam anAvilam /
   hatvā virāgaṃ rāgeṇa sarvasaukhyaṃ dadanti hi //	hatvA virAgam rAgeNa sarva sOKyam dadanti hi //
   I.1.9 Vajrasadhu	I.1.9 VajrasaDu
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   prāmodyarājamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma	prAmodya rAja mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava sattva aDizWAna vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatapramodasamayannāma	samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAgata pramoda samayat nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrasādhu //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra sADu //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sādhukārāṇi bhūtvā, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	vajraDaraH sADu kArANi BUtvA, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   praviṣṭvaikaghano bhūtvā, vajratuṣṭivigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau	pravizwvA eka GanaH BUtvA, vajra tuzwi vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO
   pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajratuṣṭivigrahāt	pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra tuzwi vigrahAt 
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāḥ tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   sarvatathāgatasādhukārādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	sarva taTAgata sADu kAra AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   suprāmodyatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanaḥ	su prAmodya tvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   prāmodyarājamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya	prAmodya rAja mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya
   tathāgatasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	taTAgatasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sādhukāro 'haṃ sarvaḥ sarvavidāṃ varaḥ /	aho hi sADukAraH aham sarvaH sarva vidAm varaH /
   yad vikalpaprahīṇānāṃ tuṣṭiṃ janayati dhruvaṃ //	yat vikalpa prahINAnAm tuzwim janayati Druvam //
   atha sa prāmodyarājamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato vairocanasya	aTa sa prAmodya rAja mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH vErocanasya
   hṛdayādavatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	hRdayAt avatIrya, sarva taTAgatAnAm pRzWatas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa //	punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasaṃtoṣaṇavajrannāma samādhiṃ saṃpādya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata saMtozaNa vajrat nAma samADim saMpAdya,
   sarvatathāgatānuttaraprāmodyajñānasamayaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvasattvasantoṣaṇamahāsukhasaumanasyānubhavanārtha	sarva taTAgata anuttara prAmodya jQAna samaya SezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva sattva santozaNa mahA suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTa
   yāvat	yAvat 
   sarvatathāgatānuttaraharṣarasottamasiddhiprāptiphalahetostadvajratuṣṭiṃ	sarva taTAgata anuttara harza rasa uttama sidDi prApti Pala hetoH tad vajra tuzwim
   tasmai prāmodyarājāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt /	tasmE prAmodya rAjAya mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt /
   tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajraharṣo vajraharṣa iti	tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajra harzaH vajraharzaH iti
   vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajraharṣo bodhisattvastena vajratuṣṭinā sarvatathāgatān sādhukāraiḥ	aTa vajraharzaH boDisattvaH tena vajra tuzwinA sarva taTAgatAn sADukArEH
   praharṣayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	praharzayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ sādhukārapravartakaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm sADu kAra pravartakam /
   sarvatuṣṭikaraṃ vajraṃ divyaṃ prāmodyavardhanam // iti //	sarva tuzwi karam vajram divyam prAmodya varDanam // iti //
   mahābodhicittaṃ, sarvatathāgatakarṣaṇasamayaḥ,	mahAboDi cittaM, sarva taTAgata karzaNa samayaH,
   sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇajñānaṃ, mahātuṣṭiriti	sarva taTAgata anurAgaNa jQAnan, mahAtuzwiH iti
   sarvatathāgatamahāsamayasattvāḥ //	sarva taTAgata mahA samaya sattvAH //
   I.1.10 Vajraratna	I.1.10 Vajra ratna
   atha bhagavān	aTa BagavAn
   punarapyākāśagarbhamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma	punar api AkASa garBa mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava ratna aDizWAna vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatābhiṣekasamayannāma	samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAgata aBizeka samayat nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajraratnaḥ //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra ratnaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH
   sarvākāśasamatājñānasuprativedhatvād, vajrasattvasamādheḥ sa eva bhagavān	sarva AkASa samatA jQAna su prativeDa tvAd, vajra sattva samADeH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvākāśarasamayo bhūtvā viniḥsṛtās, taiḥ sarvaiḥ	vajraDaraH sarva AkASa rasa mayaH BUtvA viniHsRtA as, tEH sarvEH
   sarvākāśaraśmibhiḥ sarvalokadhātavo 'vabhāsitāḥ, sarvākāśadhātusamāḥ	sarva AkASa raSmiBiH sarva loka DAtavaH avaBAsitAH, sarva AkASa DAtu samAH
   saṃvṛtā abhūvan / atha sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvo	saMvRtAH aBUvan / aTa sarva taTAgata aDizWAnena sarvaH 
   'sākāśadhāturbhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭāḥ / suparibhāvitatvācca	asa AkASa DAtuH BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwAH / su pariBAvita tvAt ca
   vajrasattvasamādheḥ sarvākāśadhātugarbhamayaḥ	vajra sattva samADeH sarva AkASa DAtu garBa mayaH
   sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajraratnavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	sarva loka DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH mahA vajra ratna vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tasmād vajraratnavigrahāt	BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tasmAt vajra ratna vigrahAt
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahāḥ prādurbhūya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH prAdurBUya,
   sarvatathāgatābhiṣekādīni sarvatathāgatarddhivikurvitāni sarvalokadhātuṣu	sarva taTAgata aBizeka AdIni sarva taTAgata RdDi vikurvitAni sarva loka DAtuzu
   kṛtvā, sarvākāśadhātugarbhasusaṃbhavatvādvajrasattvasamādheḥ	kRtvA, sarva AkASa DAtu garBasu saMBava tvAt vajra sattva samADeH
   sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ ākāśagarbhamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH AkASa garBa mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi svabhiṣeko 'haṃ vajraratnamanuttaraṃ /	aho hi su aBizekaH aham vajra ratnam anuttaram /
   yanniḥsaṃgā api jināstridhātupatayaḥ smṛtāḥ //	yat niHsaMgAH api jinAH tri DAtu patayaH smRtAH //
   atha sa ākāśagarbhamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa saH AkASa garBa mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm puratas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa //	mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatamaṇiratnavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata maNi ratnavajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatābhiprāyaparipūrṇasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvārthapariprāptisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata aBiprAya paripUrNa samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva arTa pariprApti sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgatārthasaṃpaduttamasiddhiprāptyai taṃ vajramaṇiṃ tasmai	yAvat sarva taTAgata arTa saMpad uttama sidDi prAptyE tam vajramaNim tasmE
   ākāśagarbhāya mahābodhisattvāya vajraratnacakravartitve	AkASa garBAya mahA boDisattvAya vajra ratna cakravarti tve
   vajraratnāṅkurābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicya pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	vajra ratna aFkura aBizekeNa aBizicya pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajragarbho vajragarbha iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /	sarva taTAgatEH vajragarBaH vajragarBaH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH /
   atha vajragarbho mahābodhisattvastaṃ vajramaṇiṃ svābhiṣekasthāne	aTa vajragarBaH mahA boDisattvaH tam vajramaNim sva aBizeka sTAne
   sthāpayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sTApayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sattvadhātvabhiṣecanaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm sattva DAtu aBizecanam /
   ahammama kare dattaṃ ratne ratnanniyojitaṃ //	aham mama kare dattam ratne ratnat niyojitam //
   I.1.11 Vajrateja	I.1.11 Vajrateja
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   mahātejamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma samādhiṃ	mahA teja mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava ratna aDizWAnavajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadyadaṃ sarvatathāgataraśmisamayannāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samApad yadam sarva taTAgata raSmi samayat nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrateja //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajratejaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajrapāṇiḥ mahāsūryamaṇḍalāni bhūtvā, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	vajrapANiH mahA sUrya maNxalAni BUtvA, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrasūryavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau	pravizwvA eka GanaH vajra sUrya vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO
   pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato	pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   vajrasūryamaṇḍalātsarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāḥ tathāgatavigrahā	vajra sUrya maNxalAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgataraśmipramuñcanādīni	viniHsRtya, sarva taTAgata raSmi pramuQcana AdIni
   sarvatathāgatarddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sumahātejastvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ	sarva taTAgata RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA, su mahA tejaH tvAt vajra sattva samADeH
   sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghano mahātejamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH mahA teja mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyanupamaṃ tejaḥ sattvadhātvavabhāsanaṃ /	aho hi anupamam tejaH sattva DAtu avaBAsanam /
   yacchodhayati śuddhānāṃ buddhānāmapi tāyināṃ /	yat SoDayati SudDAnAm budDAnAm api tAyinAm /
   atha sa vimalatejamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sa vimala teja mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm dakziNa candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa //	mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgataprabhāmaṇḍalādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma samādhiṃ	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata praBA maNxala aDizWAna vajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadya,	samApadya,
   sarvatathāgataraśmisamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātvanupamatejaḥsarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata raSmi samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu anupama tejaH sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvatsarvatathāgatasvayaṃprabhāvāptyuttamasiddhaye tadvajrasūryaṃ tasmai	yAvat sarva taTAgata svayaMpraBAva apti uttama sidDaye tad vajra sUryam tasmE
   mahātejase mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	mahA tejase mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajraprabho vajraprabha iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatEH vajra praBaH vajrapraBaH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajraprabho mahābodhisattvastena vajrasūryeṇa	aTa vajrapraBaH mahA boDisattvaH tena vajra sUryeNa
   sarvatathāgatānavabhāsayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sarva taTAgatAn avaBAsayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāmajñānadhvāntanāśanaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm ajQAna DvAnta nASanam /
   paramāṇurajaḥsaṃkhyasūryādhikataraprabham // iti //	paramANu rajaH saMKya sUrya aDikatara praBam // iti //
   I.1.12 Vajraketu	I.1.12 Vajraketu
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   ratnaketumahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma samādhiṃ	ratnaketu mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava ratna aDizWAnavajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatāśāparipūraṇasamayannāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samApadya idam sarva taTAgata ASA paripUraNa samayat nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajraketu //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajraketu //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharo vicitravarṇarūpālaṅkārasaṃsthānāḥ patākā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya,	vajraDaraH vicitra varNa rUpa alaFkAra saMsTAnAH patAkAH BUtvA viniHsRtya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajradhvajavigrahaḥ	BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH vajra Dvaja vigrahaH
   prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajradhvajavigrahāt	prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra Dvaja vigrahAt
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniScaritvA,
   sarvatathāgataratnadhvajocchrepaṇādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	sarva taTAgata ratna Dvaja ucCrepaNa AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   mahāratnaketutvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sadṛḍhatvāccaikaghano	mahA ratna ketu tvAt vajra sattva samADeH sa dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH 
   ratnaketumahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya	ratnaketu mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya
   tathāgatasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	taTAgatasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyasadṛśaḥ keturahaṃ sarvārthasiddhīnāṃ /	aho hi asadRSaH ketuH aham sarva arTa sidDInAm /
   yatsarvāśāparipūrṇānāṃ sarvārthapratipūraṇaṃ // iti //	yat sarva ASA paripUrNAnAm sarva arTa pratipUraNam // iti //
   atha sa ratnaketurmahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sa ratnaketuH mahAboDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa	sarva taTAgatAnAm vAma candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatocchrayādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata ucCraya aDizWAna vajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatacintārājamaṇidhvajocchrepaṇasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvāśāparipūrisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata cintA rAja maNi Dvaja ucCrepaNa samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva ASA paripUri sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgatamahārthottamasiddhiprāptiphalahetoḥ tadvajradhvajaṃ	yAvat sarva taTAgata mahA arTa uttama sidDi prApti Pala hetoH tad vajra Dvajam
   tasmai ratnaketave mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	tasmE ratna ketave mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajrayaṣṭirvajrayaṣṭiriti vajranāmabhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /	sarva taTAgatEH vajra yazwiH vajra yazwiH iti vajranAm aBizekeNa aBiziktaH /
   atha vajrayaṣṭirbodhisattvo mahāsattvastena vajradhvajena sarvatathāgatān	aTa vajra yazwiH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tena vajra Dvajena sarva taTAgatAn
   dānapāramitāyānniyojayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	dAna pAramitAyAt niyojayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ sarvāśāpaparipūraṇaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm sarva ASApa paripUraNam /
   cintāmaṇidhvajannāma dānapāramitānayam // iti //	cintAmaNiDvajan nAma dAna pAramitA anayam // iti //
   I.1.13 Vajrahasa	I.1.13 Vajrahasa
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   nityaprītipramuditendriyamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma	nitya prIti pramudita indriya mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava ratna aDizWAna vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgataprītisamayannāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAgata prIti samayat nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrahāsa //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrahAsa //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasmitāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata smitAni BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrasmitavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH vajra smita vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   prāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajrasmitavigrahāt	prANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra smita vigrahAt 
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahāḥ sarvatathāgatādbhūtādīni	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH sarva taTAgatAt BUta AdIni
   sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, nityaprītipramuditendriyatvād	sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA, nitya prIti pramudita indriya tvAt 
   vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghano	vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH 
   nityaprītipramuditendriyamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	nitya prIti pramudita indriya mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho mahāhāsamahaṃ sarvāgryāṇāṃ mahādbhutaṃ /	aho mahA hAsam aham sarva agryANAm mahA adButam /
   yatprayuñjanti buddhārthe sadaiva susamāhitāḥ //	yat prayuQjanti budDa arTe sadA eva su samAhitAH //
   atha sa nityaprītipramuditendriyamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato	aTa sa nitya prIti pramudita indriya mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH 
   hṛdayādavatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	hRdayAt avatIrya, sarva taTAgatAnAm pRzWatas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa //	punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatādbhutādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata adButa aDizWAna vajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatādbhutotpādasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvendriyānuttarasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata adButa utpAda samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva indriya anuttara suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat	yAvat 
   sarvatathāgatendriyapariśodhanajñānābhijñāvāptiphalahetostadvajrasmitaṃ	sarva taTAgata indriya pariSoDana jQAna aBijQA avApti Pala hetoH tad vajra smitam
   tasmai nityaprītipramuditendriyāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva	tasmE nitya prIti pramudita indriyAya mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva
   pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajraprītirvajraprītiriti	pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajra prItiH vajra prItiH iti
   vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajraprītirbodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ tena vajrasmitena sarvatathāgatān	aTa vajra prItiH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tena vajra smitena sarva taTAgatAn
   praharṣayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	praharzayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idantatsarvabuddhānāmadbhutotpādadarśakaṃ /	idantat sarva budDAnAm adButa utpAda darSakam /
   mahāharṣakaraṃ jñānamajñātaṃ paraśāsibhir // iti //	mahA harza karam jQAnam ajQAtam para SAsiBiH // iti //
   mahābhiṣekaḥ, vyāmaprabhāmaṇḍalaṃ, mahāsattvārtho, mahāharṣaśceti /	mahA aBizekaH, vyAma praBA maNxalaM, mahAsattva arTo, mahA harzaH ca iti /
   sarvatathāgatamahābhiṣekasattvāḥ //	sarva taTAgata mahA aBizeka sattvAH //
   I.1.14 Vajradharma	I.1.14 Vajra Darma
   atha bhagavān	aTa BagavAn
   punarapyavalokiteśvaramahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma	punar api avalokita ISvara mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava Darma aDizWAna vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgadharmasamayannāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAga Darma samayat nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajradharma //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra DarmaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ svabhāvaśuddhadharmasamatājñānasuprativedhatvāt	vajraDaraH svaBAva SudDa Darma samatA jQAna su prativeDa tvAt
   vajrasattvasamādheḥ saddharmaraśmayo bhūtvā viniścaritaḥ, taiḥ	vajra sattva samADeH sadDarma raSmayaH BUtvA viniScaritaH, tEH
   saddharmaraśmibhiḥ sarvalokadhātavo 'vabhāsitāḥ, dharmadhātumayāḥ saṃvṛtā	sadDarma raSmiBiH sarva loka DAtavaH avaBAsitAH, DarmaDAtu mayAH saMvRtA
   abhūvan / sa ca sakalo dharmadhāturbhagavato varocanasya hṛdaye	aBUvan / sa ca sakalaH DarmaDAtuH BagavataH varocanasya hRdaye
   praviṣṭvaikaghanaḥ sarvākāśadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāpadmavigrahaḥ	pravizwvA eka GanaH sarva AkASa DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH mahApadma vigrahaH
   prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tasmād	prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tasmAt 
   vajrapadmavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā	vajra padma vigrahAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānābhijñādīni	viniHsRtya, sarva taTAgata samADi jQAna aBijQA AdIni
   sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni sarvalokadhātuṣu kṛtvā, svavalokanaisvaryatvād	sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni sarva loka DAtuzu kRtvA, su avaloka nEsvarya tvAt 
   vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ	vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   avalokiteśvaramahābodhisattvakāyaḥsaṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya	avalokita ISvara mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya
   tathāgatasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	taTAgatasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi paramārtho 'hamādiśuddhaḥ svayaṃbhuvān /	aho hi parama arTaH aham AdiSudDaH svayaMBuvAn /
   yatkolopamadharmāṇāṃ viśuddhirupalabhyate //	yad kola upama DarmANAm viSudDiH upalaByate //
   atha so 'valokiteśvaramahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato vairocanasya	aTa saH avalokita ISvara mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH vErocanasya
   hṛdayādavatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	hRdayAt avatIrya, sarva taTAgatAnAm puratas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa //	punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānasamayavajrannāma samādhiṃ	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata samADi jQAna samaya vajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadya,	samApadya,
   sarvatathāgataviśodhanasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvātmapariśuddhisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata viSoDana samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva Atma pariSudDi sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgatadharmajñānābhijñāvāptiphalahetostadvajrapadmaṃ tasma	yAvat sarva taTAgata Darma jQAna aBijQA avApti Pala hetoH tad vajra padmam tasma
   avalokiteśvarāya mahābodhisattvāya saddharmacakravartitve	avalokita ISvarAya mahA boDisattvAya sat Darma cakravarti tve
   sarvatathāgatadharmakāyābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicya, pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	sarva taTAgata Darma kAya aBizekeNa aBizicya, pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatarvajranetro vajranetra iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatarvajra netraH vajra netraH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajranetro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ tadvajrapadmaṃ patravikāsanatayā	aTa vajra netraH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tad vajra padmam patra vikAsana tayA
   rāgaviśuddhinirlepasvabhāvāvalokanatathāvalokayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	rAga viSudDi nirlepa svaBAva avalokana taTA avalokayan= idamudAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ rāgatattvāvabodhanaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm rAga tattva avaboDanam /
   ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ dharma dharme pratiṣṭhitam // iti //	aham mama kare dattam Darma Darme pratizWitam // iti //
   I.1.15 Vajratiksna	I.1.15 Vajratiksna
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ	maQjuSrImahAboDisattva samayasaMBavaDarma aDizWAnavajram nAma samADim
   samāpadyadaṃ sarvatathāgatamahāprajñājñānasamayannāma	samApad yadam sarva taTAgata mahA prajQA jQAna samayannAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajratīkṣṇa //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra tIkzNaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ prajñāśastrāṇi bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya	vajraDaraH prajQA SastrANi BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH vErocanasya
   hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikadhano vajrakośavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau	hRdaye pravizwvA eka DanaH vajra koSa vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO
   pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajrakośavigrahāt	pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra koSa vigrahAt
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniScaritvA,
   sarvatathāgataprajñājñānādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	sarva taTAgata prajQA jQAna AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   sumañjuśriyatvāt vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghano	sumaQju SriyatvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH 
   mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	maQjuSrI mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa //	sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa //
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ mañjughoṣamahaṃ smṛtaḥ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm maQjuGozam aham smRtaH /
   yatprajñāyā arūpiṇyā ghoṣatvamupalabhyate //	yat prajQAyAH arUpiNyA Goza tvam upalaByate //
   atha sa mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sa maQjuSrI mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm dakziNa candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa //	mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgataprajñājñānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarvataTAgataprajQA ajQAnavajram nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatakleśacchedanasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvaduḥkhacchedanasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata kleSa= Cedana samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva duHKa= Cedana sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgataghoṣānugaprajñāpārirpūryuttamasiddhyarthaṃ tasmai	yAvat sarva taTAgata Goza anuga prajQApArirpUri uttam asidDi arTam tasmE
   mañjuśriye mahābodhisattvāya tadvajrakośaṃ tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt /	maQju Sriye mahA boDisattvAya tat vajra koSam taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt /
   tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajrabuddhirvajrabuddhiriti	tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajra budDiH vajra budDiH iti
   vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ // atha sa vajrabuddhirbodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ	vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH // aTa sa vajra budDiH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH
   tena vajrakośena sarvatathāgatān praharannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	tena vajra koSena sarva taTAgatAn praharan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ prajñāpāramitānayaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm prajQApAramitA anayam /
   chettāraṃ sarvaśatrūṇāṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ param // iti //	CettAram sarva SatrUNAm sarva pApa haram param // iti //
   I.1.16 Vajrahetu	I.1.16 Vajra hetu
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartimahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ	saha citta utpAdita Darma cakra pravarti mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava Darma aDizWAna vajram
   nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatacakrasamayannāma	nAma samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAgata cakra samayat nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrahetu //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra hetu //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharo vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalādīni sarvatathāgatamaṇḍalāni bhūtvā	vajraDaraH vajra DAtu mahA maNxala AdIni sarva taTAgata maNxalAni BUtvA
   viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano	viniHsRtya, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH 
   vajracakravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato	vajra cakra vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   vajracakravigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāḥ tathāgatavigrahā	vajra cakra vigrahAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniścaritvā, sahacittotpādadharmacakrapravartanādīni	viniScaritvA, saha citta utpAda Darma cakra pravartana AdIni
   sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni sarvalokadhātuṣu kṛtvā,	sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni sarva loka DAtuzu kRtvA,
   sahacittotpādadharmacakrapravartanatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ	saha citta utpAda Darma cakra pravartana tvAt vajra sattva samADeH
   sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ	su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya,	saha citta utpAdita Darma cakra pravarti mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho vajramayaṃ cakramahaṃ vajrāgradharmiṇām /	aho vajra mayam cakram aham vajra agra DarmiNAm /
   yaccittotpādamātreṇa dharmacakraṃ pravartate //	yat citta utpAda mAtreNa Darma cakram pravartate //
   atha sa sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartimahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato	aTa sa saha citta utpAdita Darma cakra pravarti mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH 
   hṛdayādavatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	hRdayAt avatIrya, sarva taTAgatAnAm vAma candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa //	punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatacakravajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata cakravajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatamahāmaṇḍalasamayaṃ	sarva taTAgata mahA maNxala samayam
   śeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātupraveśāvaivartikacakrasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	SezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu praveSa avEvartika cakra sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvat sarvatathāgatasaddharmacakrapravartanottamasiddhinimittaṃ	yAvat sarva taTAgata sad Darma cakra pravartana uttama sidDi nimittam
   tadvajracakraṃ tasmai sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartine	tat vajra cakram tasmE saha citta utpAdita Darma cakra pravartine
   mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajramaṇḍo vajramaṇḍa iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatEH vajramaNxaH vajramaNxaH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajramaṇḍo bodhisattvo sahāsattvastena vajracakreṇa	aTa vajramaNxaH boDisattvaH saha asattvaH tena vajra cakreNa
   sarvatathāgatānavaivartikatve pratiṣṭhāpayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sarva taTAgatAna vEvartika tve pratizWApayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sarvadharmaviśodhakam /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm sarva Darma viSoDakam /
   avaivartikacakrantu bodhimaṇḍamiti smṛtam // iti //	avEvartika cakrantu boDimaNxam iti smRtam // iti //
   I.1.17 Vajrabhasa	I.1.17 VajraBasa
   atha bhagavānavācamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma	aTa BagavAn avAca mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava Darma aDizWAna vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatajāpasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samADim samApadya idam sarvataTAgata jApa samayam nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrabhāṣa //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra BAza //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatadharmākṣarāṇi bhūtvā viniḥ sṛtya, bhagavato	vajrapANiH sarva taTAgata Darma akzarANi BUtvA viniH sRtya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikadhano vajrajāpavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka DanaH vajra jApa vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato	BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   vajrajāpavigrahātsarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā	vajra jApa vigrahAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatadharmatādini sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā	viniHsRtya, sarva taTAgata DarmatA Adini sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA
   svavācatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ	sva vAca tvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   avācamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	avAca mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   sthitvedamudānayāmāsa /	sTitvA idam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho svayaṃbhuvāṃ guhyaṃ sandhābhāṣamahaṃ smṛtaḥ /	aho svayaMBuvAm guhyam sanDA BAzam aham smRtaH /
   yad deśayanti saddharmaṃ vākprapañcavivarjitaṃ //	yat deSayanti sadDarmam vAc prapaQca vivarjitam //
   atha sa avācamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sa avAca mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm pRzWatas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa /	mArgayAmAsa /
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgataguhyavāgvajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata guhyavAc vajram nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatavāgjñānasamayaṃ	sarva taTAgata vAc jQAna samayam
   aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuvāksiddhisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu vAc sidDi sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvatsarvatathāgatavāgguhyatāprāptyuttamasiddhaye tadvajrajāpaṃ tasmai	yAvat sarva taTAgata vAc guhyata aprApti uttama sidDaye tat vajra jApam tasmE
   avācāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	avAcAya mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajravāco vajravāca iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatEH vajra vAcaH vajra vAcaH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajravāco bodhisattvo mahāsattvastena vajrajāpena sarvatathāgatān	aTa vajra vAcaH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tena vajra jApena sarva taTAgatAn
   saṃllāpayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	saM= lApayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ vajrajāpamudāhṛtaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm vajra jApam udAhRtam /
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ tu mantrāṇāmāśusādhanam // iti //	sarva taTAgatAnAm tu mantrANAm ASu sADanam // iti //
   vajradharmatājñānaṃ, sarvatathāgataprajñājñānaṃ,	vajra Darma tA jQAnaM, sarva taTAgata prajQA jQAnaM,
   mahācakrapravartanajñānaṃ, sarvatathāgatavākprapañcavinivartanajñānaṃ ceti	mahA cakra pravartana jQAnaM, sarva taTAgata vAc prapaQca vinivartana jQAnam ca iti
   / sarvatathāgatamahājñānasattvāḥ //	/ sarva taTAgata mahA jQAna sattvAH //
   I.1.18 Vajrakarma	I.1.18 Vajra karma
   atha bhagavān	aTa BagavAn
   sarvatathāgataviśvakarmamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ	sarva taTAgata viSvakarma mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava karma aDizWAna vajram
   nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, idaṃ sarvatathāgatakarmasamayannāma	nAma samADim samApadya, idam sarva taTAgata karma samayat nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrakarma //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra karma //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH
   sarvakarmasamatājñānasuprativedhatvāt vajrasattvasamādheḥ sa eva bhagavan	sarva karma sama tA jQAna su prativeDa tvAt vajra sattva samADeH saH eva Bagavan
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmasamayo bhūtvā viniḥsṛtaḥ, taiśca	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata karma samayaH BUtvA viniHsRtaH, tEH ca
   sarvatathāgatakarmaraśmibhiḥ sarvalokadhātavo bhāsitāḥ,	sarva taTAgata karma raSmiBiH sarva loka DAtavaH BAsitAH,
   sarvatathāgatakarmadhātumayāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ, sa sakalaḥ	sarva taTAgata karma DAtu mayAH saMvRttAH, sa sakalaH
   sarvatathāgatakarmadhāturbhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghanaḥ	sarva taTAgata karma DAtuH BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH
   sarvākāśadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇastataḥ sarvatathāgatakarmadhātutaḥ	sarva AkASa DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH tatas sarva taTAgata karma DAtutaH
   karmavajravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tataḥ	karma vajra vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   karmavajravigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā	karma vajra vigrahAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniḥsṛtya, sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvatathāgatakarmādīni	viniHsRtya, sarva loka DAtuzu sarva taTAgata karma AdIni
   sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   sarvatathāgatānantakarmatvādvajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ	sarva taTAgata ananta karma tvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   sarvatathāgataviśvakarmamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	sarva taTAgata viSvakarma mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyamoghaṃ buddhānāṃ sarvakarmamahaṃ bahu /	aho hi amoGam budDAnAm sarva karmam aham bahu /
   yadanābhogabuddhārthaṃ vajrakarma pravartate //	yat anABoga budDa arTam vajra karma pravartate //
   atha sa sarvatathāgataviśvakarmamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato	aTa sa sarva taTAgata viSvakarma mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH 
   hṛdayādavatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	hRdayAt avatIrya, sarva taTAgatAnAm puratas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa //	punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatāmoghavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgatAmoGavajram nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatapūjāpravartanādyaprameyāmoghasarvakarmavidhivistarasamayaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvakarmasiddhisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata pUjA pravartana Adi aprameya amoGa sarva karma viDi vistara samaya SezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva karma sidDi sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBa
   yāvat	yAvat 
   sarvatathāgatavajrakarmatājñānābhijñottamasiddhiphalahetostatkarmavajraṃ	sarva taTAgata vajra karmatA jQAna aBijQa uttama sidDi Pala hetoH tad karma vajram
   tasmai sarvatathāgataviśvakarmaṇe mahābodhisattvāya	tasmE sarva taTAgata viSvakarmaNe mahA boDisattvAya
   sarvakarmacakravartitve sarvatathāgatavajrābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicya,	sarva karma cakravarti tve sarva taTAgata vajra aBizekeNa aBizicya,
   pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajraviśvo vajraviśva iti	pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajra viSvaH vajra viSvaH iti
   vajramahābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /	vajra mahA aBizekeNa aBiziktaH /
   atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsatvastadvajraṃ svahṛdi sthāpya,	aTa vajra viSvaH boDisattvaH mahAsatvaH tat vajram sva hRdi sTApya,
   sarvatathāgatakarmatāyānniyojayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sarva taTAgata karma tAyAt niyojayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ viśvakarmakaraṃ paraṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm viSvakarma karam param /
   ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ viśve viśvaṃ niyojitam // iti //	aham mama kare dattam viSve viSvam niyojitam // iti //
   I.1.19 Vajraraksa	I.1.19 Vajra raksa
   atha bhagavān	aTa BagavAn
   duryodhanavīryamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma	duryoDana vIrya mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava karma aDizWAna vajram nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatarakṣāsamayannāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samADim samApadya idam sarva taTAgata rakzA samayat nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrarakṣa //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrarakzaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajrapāṇirdṛḍhakavacāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	vajrapANiH dRXa kavacAni BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   praviṣṭvaikaghano mahāvajrakavacavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau	pravizwvA eka GanaH mahA vajra kavaca vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH pANO
   pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato	pratizWitaH / aTa tatas 
   vajrakavacavigrahātsarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā	vajra kavaca vigrahAt sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahA
   viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatarakṣāvidhivistarakarmādīni	viniHsRtya, sarva taTAgata rakzA viDi vistara karma AdIni
   sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, duryodhanavīryatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ	sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA, duryoDana vIrya tvAt vajra sattva samADeH
   sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghano duryodhanavīryamahābodhisattvavigrahaḥ saṃbhūya,	su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH duryoDana vIrya mahA boDisattva vigrahaH saMBUya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho vīryamayo varmaḥ sudṛḍho 'haṃ dṛḍhātmanāṃ /	aho vIrya mayaH varmaH su dRXaH aham dRXa AtmanAm /
   yad dṛḍhatvādakāyānāṃ vajrakāyakaraṃ paraṃ //	yat dRXa tvAt akAyAnAm vajra kAya karam param //
   atha sa duryodhanavīryamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sa duryoDana vIrya mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūttvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm dakziNa candra maNxala ASritaH BUt tvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa //	mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatadṛḍhavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata dRXavajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatavīryapāramitāsamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata vIrya pAramitA samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu paritrANa sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvatsarvatathāgatavajrakāyaprāptyuttamasiddhihetostadvajravarma tasmai	yAvat sarva taTAgata vajra kAya prApti uttama sidDi hetoH tat vajra varma tasmE
   duryodhanavīryāya mahābodhisattvāya pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt / tataḥ	duryoDana vIryAya mahA boDisattvAya pANiByAm anuprAdAt / tatas 
   sarvatathāgatairvajramitro vajramitra iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	sarva taTAgatEH vajramitraH vajramitraH iti vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajramitro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ tena vajravarmeṇa sarvatathāgatān	aTa vajramitraH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tena vajra varmeNa sarva taTAgatAn
   kavacayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	kavacayan= idamudAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ maitrīkavacamuttamaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm mEtrI kavacam uttamam /
   dṛḍhavīryamahārakṣaṃ mahāmitramudāhṛtama // iti //	dRXa vIrya mahArakzam mahA mitram udAhRtame // iti //
   I.1.20 Vajrayaksa	I.1.20 Vajrayak sa
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvamārapramārdemahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajrannāma	sarva mAra pramArdemahA boDisattva samaya saMBava karma aDizWAna vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatopāyasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ	samADim samApadya idam sarvataTAgata upAya samayam nAma sarva taTAgata hRdayam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrayakṣa //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrayakza //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharo mahādaṃṣṭrāyudhāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya	vajraDaraH mahA daMzwra AyuDAni BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH vErocanasya
   hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajradaṃṣṭrāvigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, pāṇau	hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH vajra daMzwrA vigrahaH prAdurBUya, pANO
   pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajradaṃṣṭrāvigrahāt	pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra daMzwrA vigrahAt
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniScaritvA,
   sarvatathāgataraudravinayādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā,	sarva taTAgata rOdra vinaya AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni kRtvA,
   sarvamārasupramarditvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ	sarva mArasu pramardi tvAt vajra sattva samADeH su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH
   sarvamārapramardimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya	sarva mAra pramardi mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya
   hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa //	hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa //
   aho mahopāyamahaṃ buddhānāṃ karuṇātmanāṃ /	aho mahA upAyam aham budDAnAm karuNa AtmanAm /
   yatsattvārthatayā śāntā raudratvamapi kuruvate //	yat sattva arTa tayA SAntA rOdra tvam api kuruvate //
   atha sa sarvamārapramardimahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sa sarva mAra pramardi mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ mārgayāmāsa	sarva taTAgatAnAm vAma candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm mArgayAmAsa
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatapracaṇḍavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata pracaNxavajrad nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgataduṣṭavinayasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣatvadhātvabhayasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata duzwa vinaya samayam aSezAn avaSeza tva DAtu aBaya sarva suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvatsarvatathāgatamahopāyajñānābhijñāvāptyuttamasiddhiphalahetostadvajradaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ	yAvat sarva taTAgata mahA upAya jQAna aBijQA vApti uttama sidDi Pala hetoH tad vajra daMzwra AyuDam
   tasmai sarvamārapramardine mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt /	tasmE sarva mAra pramardine mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt /
   tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajracaṇḍo vajracaṇḍa iti	tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajracaNxaH vajracaNxaH iti
   vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha vajracaṇḍo bodhisattvo mahāsattvastadvajradaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ svamukhe	aTa vajracaNxaH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tad vajra daMzwra AyuDam sva muKe
   pratiṣṭhāpya, sarvatathāgatān bhīṣayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	pratizWApya, sarva taTAgatAn BIzayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sarvaduṣṭāgradāmakaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm sarva duzwa agra dAmakam /
   vajradaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ tīkṣṇamupāyaḥ karūṇātmanām // iti //	vajra daMzwra AyuDam tIkzNam upAyaH karUNa AtmanAm // iti //
   I.1.21 Vajrasandhi	I.1.21 Vajra sanDi
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvatathāgatamuṣṭimahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma	sarva taTAgata muzwi mahA boDisattva samaya saMBava karma aDizWAna vajram nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyadaṃ sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajrabandhasamayannāma	samADim samApad yadam sarva taTAgatakAya vAc citta vajra banDa samayat nAma
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrasandhi //	sarva taTAgata hRdayam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra sanDi //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvamudrābandhā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata sarva mudrA banDAH BUtvA viniHsRtya, BagavataH 
   vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrabandhavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	vErocanasya hRdaye pravizwvA eka GanaH vajra banDa vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ / atha tato vajrabandhavigrahāt	pANO pratizWitaH / aTa tatas vajra banDa vigrahAt 
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniScaritvA,
   sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvatathāgatamudrājñānādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni	sarva loka DAtuzu sarva taTAgata mudrA jQAna AdIni sarva budDa RdDi vikurvitAni
   kṛtvā, sarvatathāgatamahāmuṣṭisubandhatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ	kRtvA, sarva taTAgata mahA muzwi subanDa tvAt vajra sattva samADeH
   sudṛḍhatvāccaikaghanaḥ sarvatathāgatamuṣṭimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya,	su dRXa tvAt ca eka GanaH sarva taTAgata muzwi mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye sTitvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sudṛḍho bandhaḥ samayo 'haṃ dṛḍhātmanāṃ /	aho hi su dRXaH banDaH samayaH aham dRXa AtmanAm /
   yatsarvāśāprasiddhyarthaṃ muktānāmapi bandhanaṃ //	yat sarva ASA prasidDi arTam muktAnAm api banDanam //
   atha sarvatathāgatamuṣṭimahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayādavatīrya,	aTa sarva taTAgata muzwi mahA boDisattva kAyaH BagavataH hRdayAt avatIrya,
   sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punarapyājñāṃ	sarva taTAgatAnAm pRzWatas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA, punar api AjQAm
   mārgayāmāsa //	mArgayAmAsa //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamayavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya,	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgata samaya vajrat nAma samADim samApadya,
   sarvatathāgatamudrābandhasamayamaśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvatathāgatadevatāsānnidhyakalpanāt	sarva taTAgata mudrA banDa samayam aSezAn avaSeza sattva DAtu sarva taTAgata devatA sAnniDya kalpanAt 
   sarvasiddhisukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ	sarva sidDi suKa sOmanasya anuBavana arTam
   yāvatsarvatathāgatasarvajñānamudrādhipatyottamasiddhiphalahetostadvajrabandhaṃ	yAvat sarva taTAgata sarva jQAna mudrA ADipatya uttama sidDi Pala hetoH tad vajra banDam
   tasmai sarvatathāgatamuṣṭaye mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyāmanuprādāt	tasmE sarva taTAgata muzwaye mahA boDisattvAya taTA eva pANiByAm anuprAdAt 
   / tataḥ sarvatathāgatairvajramuṣṭirvajramuṣṭiriti	/ tatas sarva taTAgatEH vajramuzwiH vajramuzwiH iti
   vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //	vajra nAma aBizekeNa aBiziktaH //
   atha sa vajramuṣṭirbodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ tena vajrabandhena	aTa sa vajra muzwiH boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH tena vajra banDena
   sarvatathāgatān bandhayannidamudānamudānayāmāsa /	sarva taTAgatAn banDayan= idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   idaṃ tatsarvabuddhānāṃ mudrābandhaṃ mahādṛḍhaṃ /	idam tat sarva budDAnAm mudrA banDam mahA dRXam /
   yatsarvabuddhāśusiddhyarthaṃ samayo duratikramaḥ // iti //	yat sarva budDa ASu sidDi arTam samayaH duratikramaH // iti //
   sarvatathāgatapūjāvidhivistarakarma, mahāvīryadṛḍhakavacaḥ,	sarva taTAgata pUjA viDi vistara karma, mahA vIrya dRXa kavacaH,
   sarvatathāgatamahopāyaḥ, sarvamudrājñānaṃ ceti /	sarva taTAgata mahA upAyaH, sarva mudrA jQAnam ca iti /
   sarvatathāgatamahākarmasattvāḥ //	sarva taTAgata mahA karma sattvAH //
   I.1.22 Sattvavajri	I.1.22 Sattva vajri
   atha khalvakṣobhyastathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa Kalu akzoByaH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   sarvatathāgatajñānāni niṣpādya, sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ	sarva taTAgata jQAnAni nizpAdya, sarva taTAgata jQAna mudraNa arTam
   vajrāpāramitāsamayobhdavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ	vajrApAramitAsamayA uBdavavajrADizWAnam nAma samADim samApadya imAm
   sarvatathāgatavajrasamayāṃ nāma sarvatathāgatamudrāṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra	sarva taTAgata vajra samayAm nAma sarva taTAgata mudrAm sva hRdayAt niScacAra
   sattvavajri //	sattva vajri //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajraraśmayo	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH vajra raSmayaH 
   viniścaritāḥ /	viniScaritAH /
   tebhyaśca vajraraśmibhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	teByaH ca vajra raSmiByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA,
   sarvatathāgatavajrapāramitājñānānyāmudrya, punarapyekaghanaḥ	sarva taTAgata vajra pAramitA jQAna ani Amudrya, punar api eka GanaH
   sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	sarva loka DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH mahA vajra vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   bhagavatovairocanasya purataścandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	BagavataH vErocanasya puratas candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ sattvavajramahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm sattva vajra m aham dRXaH /
   yad dṛḍhatvādakāyo 'pi vajrakāyatvamāgataḥ // iti //	yat dRXa tvAt akAyaH api vajra kAya tvam AgataH // iti //
   I.1.23 Ratnavajri	I.1.23 Ratna vajri
   atha bhagavān ratnasaṃbhavastathāgataḥ bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa BagavAn ratna saMBavaH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ ratnapāramitāsamayasaṃbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ	sarva taTAgata jQAna mudraNa arTam ratna pAra mitA samaya saMBava vajra aDizWAnam
   nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ vajraratnasamayāṃ nāma svamudrāṃ	nAma samADim samApadya imAm vajra ratna samayAm nAma sva mudrAm
   svahṛdayānniścacāra ratnavajri //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra ratna vajri //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo ratnaraśmayo	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH ratna raSmayaH 
   viniścaritāḥ / tebhyo ratnaraśmibhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	viniScaritAH / teByaH ratna raSmiByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA,
   sarvatathāgatajñānānyāmudrya, punarapyekaghanaḥ	sarva taTAgata jQAna ani Amudrya, punar api eka GanaH
   sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajraratnavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	sarva loka DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH mahA vajra ratna vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya dakṣiṇapārśve candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	BagavataH vErocanasya dakziNa pArSve candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ ratnavajramahaṃ smṛtaṃ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm ratna vajra m aham smRtam /
   yanmudrāṇāṃ hi sarvāsāmabhiṣekanayaṃ dṛḍham // iti //	yat mudrANAm hi sarvAsAm aBizeka nayam dRXam // iti //
   I.1.24 Dharamavajri	I.1.24 Dharam avajri
