   atha bhagavān lokeśvararājastathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa BagavAn lokeSvara rAjaH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ dharmapāramitāsamayodbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ	sarva taTAgata jQAna mudraNa arTam Darma pAramitA samaya udBava vajra aDizWAnam
   nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ dharmasamayāṃ nāma svamudrāṃ	nAma samADim samApadya imAm Darma samayAm nAma sva mudrAm
   svahṛdayānniścacāra dharma vajri //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra Darma vajri //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ padmaraśmayo	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH padma raSmayaH 
   viniścaritāḥ / tebhyaḥ padmaraśmibhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	viniScaritAH / teByaH padma raSmiByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA,
   sarvatathāgatajñānānyāmudrya, punarapyekaghanaḥ	sarva taTAgata jQAna ani Amudrya, punar api eka GanaH
   sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajrapadmavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya,	sarva loka DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH mahA vajra padma vigrahaH prAdurBUya,
   bhagavato vairocanasya pṛṣṭhataścandramaṇḍalāśrito	BagavataH vErocanasya pRzWatas candra maNxala ASritaH 
   bhūtvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BUtvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ dharmavajraṃ ahaṃ śuci /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm Darma vajram aham Suci /
   yatsvabhāvaviśuddhyā vai rāgo 'pi hi sunirmalaḥ // iti //	yad svaBAva viSudDyA vE rAgaH api hi su nirmalaH // iti //
   I.1.25 Karmavajiri	I.1.25 Karmavajiri
   atha bhagavānamoghasiddhistathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa BagavAn amoGa sidDiH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ karmapāramitāsaṃbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma	sarva taTAgata jQAna mudraNa arTam karmapAramitAsaMBava vajrADizWAnam nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakarmasamayāṃ nāma svamudrāṃ	samADim samApadya imAm sarva taTAgata karma samayAm nAma sva mudrAm
   svahṛdayānniścacāra karmavajri //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra karma vajri //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvakarmaśmayo	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH sarva karma SmayaH 
   viniścaritāḥ / tebhyaśca sarvatathāgatakarmaraśmimabhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	viniScaritAH / teByaH ca sarva taTAgata karma raSmim aByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā,	vajraDaraH sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA,
   sarvatathāgatajñānānyamudrya, punarapyekaghanaḥ	sarva taTAgata jQAna ani a mudrya, punar api eka GanaH
   sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇaḥ sarvatomukho mahākarmavajravigrahaḥ	sarva loka DAtu samavasaraNa pramANaH sarvatomuKaH mahA karma vajra vigrahaH
   prādurbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya vāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā,	prAdurBUya, BagavataH vErocanasya vAma pArSve candra maNxala ASritaH BUtvA,
   idamudānamudānayāmāsa //	idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa //
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ karmavajramahaṃ bahu /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm karma vajram aham bahu /
   yadekaḥ sannaśeṣasya sattvadhātoḥ sukarmakṛd // iti //	yat ekaH sanna Sezasya sattva DAtoH su karma kRt // iti //
   sarvatathāgatajñānasamayā, mahābhiṣekā, vajradharmatā, sarvapūjā ceti /	sarva taTAgata jQAna samayA, mahA aBizekA, vajraDarma tA, sarva pUjA ca iti /
   sarvatathāgatapāramitāḥ //	sarva taTAgata pAramitAH //
   I.1.26 Vajralasya	I.1.26 Vajralasya
   atha bhagavān vairocanaḥ punarapi	aTa BagavAn vErocanaH punar api
   sarvatathāgataratipūjāsamayasaṃbhavavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ	sarva taTAgata rati pUjA samaya saMBava vajrat nAma samADim samApadya imAm
   sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajralāsye //	sarva taTAgata kula mahAdevIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra lAsye //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajramudrā viniḥsṛtāḥ	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH vajra mudrAH viniHsRtAH
   / tebhyo vajramudrāmukhabhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	/ teByaH vajra mudrA muKaByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, punarapyekaghanā	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA, punar api eka GanA
   mahādevī vajrasattvasadṛśātmabhāvā vicitravarṇarūpaliṅgeryāpathā	mahAdevI vajra sattva sadRSa Atma BAvA vicitra varNa rUpa liFgeH yApaTA
   sarvālaṅkāravibhūṣitā sarvatathāgatakulasaṃgrahabhūtā vajrasattvadayitā	sarva alaFkAra viBUzitA sarva taTAgata kula saMgraha BUtA vajra sattva dayitA
   saṃbhūya, bhagavato 'kṣobhyamaṇḍalavāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvā,	saMBUya, BagavataH akzoBya maNxala vAma pArSve candra maNxala ASritA BUtvA,
   idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho na sadṛśī me 'sti pūjā hyanyā svayaṃbhuvāṃ /	aho na sadRSI me asti pUjA hi anyA svayaMBuvAm /
   yatkāmaratipūjābhiḥ sarvapūjā pravartate // iti //	yat kAmarati pUjABiH sarva pUjA pravartate // iti //
   I.1.27 Vajramala	I.1.27 Vajra mala
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvatathāgataratnamālābhiṣekasamayodbhavavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadya	sarva taTAgata ratna mAlA aBizeka samaya udBava vajrat nAma samADim samApadya
   māṃ sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajramāle /	mAm sarva taTAgata kula mahAdevIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra mAle /
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo mahāratnamudrā	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH mahA ratna mudrA
   viniḥsṛtāḥ / tābhyo mahāratnamudrābhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	viniHsRtAH / tAByaH mahA ratna mudrAByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, ekaghanāṃ	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA, eka GanAm
   vajramālāṃ mahādevīṃ tathaiva saṃbhūya, bhagavato	vajramAlAm mahAdevIm taTA eva saMBUya, BagavataH 
   ratnasaṃbhavamaṇḍalavāmapārśve pūrṇacandramaṇḍalāśritā	ratna saMBava maNxala vAma pArSve pUrNa candra maNxala ASritA
   bhūtvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BUtvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyasadṛśāhaṃ vai ratnapūjeti kīrtitā /	aho hi asadRSA aham vE ratna pUjA iti kIrtitA /
   yattraidhātukarājyāgryaṃ śāsayanti prapūjitā // iti //	yat trEDAtuka rAjya agryam SAsayanti prapUjitAH // iti //
   I.1.28 Vajragita	I.1.28 Vajragita
   atha bhagavān punarapi sarvatathāgatasaṃgītisamayasaṃbhavavajrannāma	aTa BagavAn punar api sarva taTAgata saMgIti samaya saMBava vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra	samADim samApadya imAm sarva taTAgata kula mahAdevIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra
   vajragīte //	vajra gIte //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdaye 'bhyaḥ	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdaye aByaH
   sarvatathāgatadharmamudrā viniścaritāḥ / tābhyaśca	sarva taTAgata Darma mudrAH viniScaritAH / tAByaH ca
   sarvatathāgatadharmamudrābhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	sarva taTAgata Darma mudrAByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, punarapyekaghanāṃ	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA, punar api eka GanAm
   vajragītāṃ mahādevīṃ saṃbhūya, bhagavato lokeśvararājamaṇḍalavāmapārśve	vajra gItAm mahAdevIm saMBUya, BagavataH loka ISvara rAja maNxala vAma pArSve
   candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	candra maNxala ASritA BUtvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi saṃgītimayī pūjāhaṃ sarvadarśināṃ /	aho hi saMgIti mayI pUjA aham sarva darSinAm /
   yat toṣayanti pūjābhiḥ pratiśrutkopameṣvapi // iti //	yat tozayanti pUjABiH pratiSrutka upamezu api // iti //
   I.1.29 Vajranrtya	I.1.29 Vajranrtya
   atha bhagavān punarapi sarvatathāgatanṛtyapūjāsamayodbhavavajraṃ nāma	aTa BagavAn punar api sarvataTAgatanRtyapUjA samayodBavavajram nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra	samADim samApadya imAm sarva taTAgata kula mahAdevIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra
   vajranṛtye /	vajra nRtye /
   athāsmina viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ	aTa asmina viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH
   sarvatathāgatanṛtyapūjāvidhivistarā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ / tebhyaśca	sarva taTAgata nRtya pUjA viDi vistarAH BUtvA viniHsRtAH / teByaH ca
   sarvatathāgatasarvanṛttapūjāvidhivistarebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ	sarva taTAgata sarva nRtta pUjA viDi vistareByaH saH eva BagavAn vajraDaraH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, punarapyekaghanāṃ	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH BUtvA, punar api eka GanAm
   vajranṛttamahādevīṃ saṃbhūya, bhagavato amoghasiddhestathāgatasya	vajra nRtta mahAdevIm saMBUya, BagavataH amoGa sidDeH taTAgatasya
   maṇḍalavāmapārśve pūrṇacandramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	maNxala vAma pArSve pUrNa candra maNxala ASritA BUtvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyudārapūjāhaṃ sarvapūjārthakariṇāṃ /	aho hi udAra pUjA aham sarva pUjA arTa kariNAm /
   yadvajranṛttavidhinā buddhapūjā prakalpyate // iti //	yat vajra nRtta viDinA budDa pUjA prakalpyate // iti //
   sarvatathāgatānuttarasukhasaumanasyasamayā, sarvatathāgatamālā,	sarva taTAgata anuttara suKa sOmanasya samayA, sarva taTAgata mAlA,
   sarvatathāgatagāthā, sarvatathāgatānuttarapūjākarmakarī ceti /	sarva taTAgata gATA, sarva taTAgata anuttara pUjA karma karI ca iti /
   sarvatathāgataguhyapūjāḥ //	sarva taTAgata guhya pUjAH //
   I.1.30 Vajradhupa	I.1.30 VajraDupa
   atha punarapi bhagavān akṣobhyastathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya	aTa punar api BagavAn akzoByaH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya
   tathāgatasya pūjāpratipūjārtha	taTAgatasya pUjA pratipUjA arTa
   sarvatathāgatapralhādanasamayodbhavavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ	sarva taTAgata pralhAdana samaya udBava vajrat nAma samADim samApadya imAm
   sarvatathāgatagaṇikāṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajradhūpe //	sarva taTAgata gaNikAm sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra DUpe //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ anekavidhā dhūpapūjāmeghavyūhāḥ sarvavajradhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā	vajraDaraH anekaviDAH DUpa pUjA meGa vyUhAH sarva vajra DAtu sParaNA BUtvA
   viniścaritāḥ / tebhyaśca dhūpapūjāmeghasamudrebhyaḥ	viniScaritAH / teByaH ca DUpa pUjA meGa samudreByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   punarapyekaghano vajradhūpadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	punar api eka GanaH vajra DUpa devatA kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya koṇe vāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśritā	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya koNe vAma pArSve candra maNxala ASritA
   bhūtvedamudānamudānayati sma /	BUtvA idam udAnam udAnayati sma /
   aho hyaṃ mahāpūjā pralhādanavatī śubhā /	aho hyam mahA pUjA pralhAdanavatI SuBA /
   yatsattvāveśayogāddhi kṣipraṃ bodhiravāpyate // iti //	yat sattva AveSa yogAt hi kzipram boDiH avApyate // iti //
   I.1.31 Vajrapuspa	I.1.31 Vajra puspa
   atha bhagavān ratnasaṃbhavastathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa BagavAn ratna saMBavaH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   pūjāpratipūjārtha ratnābharaṇapūjāsamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ	pUjA pratipUjA arTa ratnABaraNa pUjAsamayasaMBavavajram nAma samADim
   samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatapratīhārīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrapuṣpe //	samApadya imAm sarva taTAgata pratIhArIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra puzpe //
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvapuṣpapūjāvyūhāḥ sarvākāśadhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā	vajraDaraH sarva puzpa pUjA vyUhAH sarva AkASa DAtu sParaNA BUtvA
   viniḥsṛtāstebhyaśca sarvapuṣpapūjāvyūhebhyaḥ	viniHsRtAH teByaH ca sarva puzpa pUjA vyUheByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   punarapyekaghano vajrapuṣpadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	punar api eka GanaH vajra puzpadevatA kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vāmakoṇe candramaṇḍalāśritā	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya vAma koNe candra maNxala ASritA
   bhūtvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BUtvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi puṣpapūjāhaṃ sarvālaṅkārakārikā /	aho hi puzpa pUjA aham sarva alaFkAra kArikAH /
   yattathāgataratnatvaṃ pūjya kṣipramavāpyate // iti //	yat taTAgata ratna tvam pUjya kzipram avApyate // iti //
   I.1.32 Vajraloka	I.1.32 Vajra loke 
   atha bhagavān lokeśvararājastathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa BagavAn lokeSvara rAjaH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   pūjāpratipūjārtha sarvatathāgatālokapūjāsamayodbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ	pUjA pratipUjA arTa sarvataTAgatAlokapUjA asamayodBavavajram nAma samADim
   samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatadūtīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrāloke /	samApadya imAm sarva taTAgata dUtIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrAloke /
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvālokapūjāvyūhāḥ sakaladharmadhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā	vajraDaraH sarva Aloka pUjA vyUhAH sakala Darma DAtu sParaNA BUtvA
   viniścaritāḥ / tebhyaśca sarvālokapūjāvyūhebhyaḥ	viniScaritAH / teByaH ca sarva Aloka pUjA vyUheByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   punarapyekaghano vajrālokadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	punar api eka GanaH vajra Aloka devatA kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vāmakoṇe candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvā,	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya vAma koNe candra maNxala ASritA BUtvA,
   idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hyahaṃ mahodārā pūjā dīpamayī śubhā /	aho hi aham mahA udArA pUjA dIpa mayI SuBA /
   yadālokavatī kṣipraṃ sarvabuddhadṛśo labhed // iti //	yat AlokavatI kzipram sarva budDa dRSaH laBet // iti //
   I.1.33 Vajragandha	I.1.33 VajraganDa
   atha bhagavānamoghasiddhistathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya	aTa BagavAn amoGa sidDiH taTAgataH BagavataH vErocanasya taTAgatasya
   pūjāpratipūjārthaṃ sarvatathāgatagandhapajāsamayasaṃbhavavajrannāma	pUjA pratipUjA arTam sarva taTAgata ganDa pajAsamaya saMBava vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgataceṭīṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajragandhe	samADim samApadya imAm sarva taTAgata cewIm sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajraganDe
   athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asyAm viniHsRta mAtrAyAm sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvagandhapūjāvyūhāḥ sarvalokadhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ	vajraDaraH sarva ganDa pUjA vyUhAH sarva loka DAtu sParaNAH BUtvA viniHsRtAH
   / tebhyaśca gandhapūjāvyūhebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥ	/ teByaH ca ganDa pUjA vyUheByaH sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH
   samāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya punarapyekaghano vajragandhadevatākāyaḥ	samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya punar api eka GanaH vajra ganDa devatA kAyaH
   saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vāmakoṇe	saMBUya, BagavataH vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya vAma koNe
   candramaṇḍalāśritā bhatvedamudānamudānayāmāsa /	candra maNxala ASritA BatvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho gandhamayī pūjā divyāhaṃ manoramā /	aho ganDa mayI pUjA divyA aham manoramA /
   yattathāgatagandho vai sarvakāye dadāti hi // iti //	yat taTAgata ganDaH vE sarva kAye dadAti hi // iti //
   sarvatathāgatajñānāveśā, mahābodhyaṅgasaṃcayā, sarvatathāgatadharmālokā,	sarva taTAgata jQAna AveSA, mahA boDi aFga saMcayA, sarva taTAgata Darma AlokA,
   śīlasamādhiprajñāvimuktivimuktijñānadarśanagandhā ceti /	SIla samADi prajQA vimukti vimukti jQAna darSana ganDA ca iti /
   sarvatathāgatājñākāryaḥ //	sarva taTAgata AjQA kAryaH //
   I.1.34 Vajrankusa	I.1.34 Vajran kusa
   atha bhagavān vairocanastathāgataḥ punarapi sarvatathāgatasamayāṃ	aTa BagavAn vErocanaH taTAgataH punar api sarva taTAgata samayAm
   kuśamahāsattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvavajrannāma samādhiṃ samāpadyeyaṃ	kuSa mahA sattva samaya saMBava sattva vajrat nAma samADim samApadyeyam
   sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāgaṇapatiṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrāṃkuśa //	sarva taTAgata sarva mudrA gaNa patim sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrAMkuSaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātra sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtra sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtaḥ / tebhyaśca	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata sarva mudrA gaNAH BUtvA viniHsRtaH / teByaH ca
   sarvatathāgatamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ	sarva taTAgata mudrA gaNeByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   punarapyekaghano vajrāṅkuśamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	punar api eka GanaH vajra aFkuSa mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vajradvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya vajra dvAra maDye candra maNxala ASritaH 
   bhatvā, sarvatathāgatasamayānākarṣayanna, idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	Ba tvA, sarva taTAgata samayAn Akarzayanna, idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ samākarṣamahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm samAkarzam aham dRXaH /
   yanmayā hi samākṛṣṭā bhajante sarvamaṇḍalam // iti //	yat mayA hi samAkRzwAH Bajante sarva maNxalam // iti //
   I.1.35 Vajrapasa	I.1.35 Vajrapasa
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvatathāgatasamayapraveśamahāsattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvavajrannāma	sarva taTAgata samaya praveSa mahA sattva samaya saMBava sattva vajrat nAma
   samādhiṃ samāpadya maṃ sarvatathāgatamudrāpraveśapratīhāraṃ	samADim samApadya mam sarva taTAgata mudrA praveSa pratIhAram
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrapāśa //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrapASaH //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayapraveśamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniścaritaḥ /	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata samaya praveSa mudrA gaNAH BUtvA viniScaritaH /
   tebhyaśca sarvatathāgatasamayapraveśamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ	teByaH ca sarva taTAgata samaya praveSa mudrA gaNeByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya,	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya,
   punarapyekaghano vajrapāśamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	punar api eka GanaH vajra pASa mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya ratnadvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya ratna dvAra maDye candra maNxala ASritaH 
   bhūtvā sarvatathāgatāṃ praveśayann, idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BUtvA sarva taTAgatAm praveSayann, idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrapāśamahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm vajra pASam aham dRXaH /
   yatsarvāṇupraviṣṭāpi praveśyante mayā punaḥ // iti //	yat sarva aNu pravizwA api praveSyante mayA punar // iti //
   I.1.36 Vajrasphota	I.1.36 VajrasPota
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvatathāgatasamayasphoṭamahāsattvasamayodbhavasattvavajrannāmasamādhiṃ	sarva taTAgata samaya sPowa mahA sattva samaya udBava sattva vajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatasamayabandhannāma sarvatathāgatadūtaṃ	samApadya imam sarva taTAgata samaya banDat nAma sarva taTAgata dUtam
   svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrasphoṭa //	sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajrasPowa //
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayabandhamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtastebhyaśca	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata samaya banDa mudrA gaNAH BUtvA viniHsRtaH teByaH ca
   sarvatathāgatasamayabandhasarvamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ	sarva taTAgata samaya banDa sarva mudrA gaNeByaH
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, ekaghano	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya, eka GanaH 
   vajrasphoṭamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato	vajra sPowa mahA boDisattva kAyaH saMBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya dharmadvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya Darma dvAra maDye candra maNxala ASritaH 
   bhatvā, sarvatathāgatāna bandhayanna, idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	Ba tvA, sarva taTAgatAna banDayanna, idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrasphoṭamahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm vajrasPowam aham dRXaH /
   yatsarvabandhamuktānāṃ sattvārthād bandha iṣyate // iti //	yat sarva banDa muktAnAm sattva arTAt banDaH izyate // iti //
   I.1.37 Vajravesa	I.1.37 Vajravesa
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvatathāgatāveśamahāsattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvavajrannāma samādhiṃ	sarva taTAgata AveSa mahA sattva samaya saMBava sattva vajrat nAma samADim
   samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāceṭaṃ svahṛdayānniścacāra vajrāveśaḥ	samApadya imam sarva taTAgata sarva mudrA cewam sva hRdayAt niScacAra vajra AveSaH
   athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān	aTa asmin viniHsRta mAtre sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH saH eva BagavAn
   vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniścaritaḥ / tebhyaśca	vajraDaraH sarva taTAgata sarva mudrA gaNAH BUtvA viniScaritaH / teByaH ca
   sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥ	sarva taTAgata sarva mudrA gaNeByaH sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH
   samāstathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, ekaghano	samAH taTAgata vigrahAH viniHsRtya, eka GanaH 
   vajrāveśamahābodhisattvavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavato	vajra AveSa mahA boDisattva vigrahaH prAdurBUya, BagavataH 
   vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya karmadvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito	vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya karma dvAra maDye candra maNxala ASritaH 
   bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatānāveśayanna, idamudānamudānayāmāsa /	BUtvA, sarva taTAgatAn AveSayat na, idam udAnam udAnayAmAsa /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrāveśamahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm vajra AveSam aham dRXaH /
   yatsarvapatayo bhūtvā ceṭā api bhavanti hi // iti //	yat sarva patayaH BUtvA cewAH api Bavanti hi // iti //
   savatathāgatasamākarṣaṇaṃ, praveśo, bandhaḥ, vaśīkaraṇaṃ ceti /	savataTA gata samAkarzaNan, praveSo, banDaH, vaSIkaraNam ca iti /
   sarvatathāgatājñākarāḥ //	sarva taTAgata AjQA karAH //
   atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatāsamājādhiṣṭhānāya vajrācchaṭikāsaṃjñāmakārṣīt	aTa BagavAn sarva taTAgatA samAja aDizWAnAya vajrAt SawikA saMjQAm akArzIt 
   / idaṃ sarvatathāgatasamājādhiṣṭhānahṛdayamabhāṣata vajrasamāja //	/ idam sarva taTAgata samAja aDizWAna hRdayam aBAzata vajra samAja //
   atha tena kṣapālavamuhūrtena sarvatathāgatācchaṭikāsaṃjñāsaṃcoditāḥ	aTa tena kzapA lava muhUrtena sarva taTAgatAt SawikA saMjQA saMcoditAH
   sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudreṣu	sarva loka DAtu prasara meGa samudrezu
   sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamāstathāgatāḥ sabodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāḥ	sarva loka DAtu paramANu rajaH samAH taTAgatAH sa boDisattva parzad maNxalAH
   samājamāpadya, yena bhagavān vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgāro yena ca	samAjam Apadya, yena BagavAn vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgAraH yena ca
   bhagavān vairocanastenopajagmurupetya oṃ sarvatathāgatapādavandanāṅkaromi	BagavAn vErocanaH tena upajagmuH upetya om sarva taTAgata pAda vandana aFkaromi
   // ityenena prakṛtisiddhena mantreṇa rucijaptena	// iti enena prakRti sidDena mantreNa ruci japtena
   sarvatathāgatapādavandanāṃ kṛtvedamudānamudānayāmāsuḥ //	sarva taTAgata pAda vandanAm kRtvA idam udAnam udAnayAmAsuH //
   aho samantabhadrasya bodhisattvasya satkriyā /	aho samantaBadrasya boDisattvasya satkriyA /
   yattathāgatacakrasya madhye bhāti tathāgataḥ //	yat taTAgata cakrasya maDye BAti taTAgataH //
   athedamuktvā te daśadiksarvalokadhātusannipatitāḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ	aTa idam uktvA te daSa diS sarva loka DAtu sannipatitAH sarva taTAgatAH
   sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye	sarva taTAgata aDizWAnena BagavataH vErocanasya hRdaye
   sabodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāḥ praviṣṭāḥ / tebhyaśca	sa boDisattva parzad maNxalAH pravizwAH / teByaH ca
   sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ svāni svāni bodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāni	sarva taTAgata hRdayeByaH svAni svAni boDisattva parzad maNxalAni
   viniḥsṛtya bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya sarvapārśveṣu	viniHsRtya BagavataH vajra maNi ratna SiKara kUwa AgArasya sarva pArSvezu
   maṇḍalībhūtvā samāpadyāvasthitā idamudānamudānayāmāsuḥ /	maNxalIBUtvA samApadya avasTitAH idam udAnam udAnayAmAsuH /
   aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ mahodāryamanādijam /	aho hi sarva budDAnAm mahA udAryam anAdi jam /
   yatsarvāṇuprasaṃkhyā vai buddhā hyekatvamāgatā // iti //	yat sarva aNu prasaMKyAH vE budDAH hi eka tvam AgatAH // iti //
   Hymn of 108 Names of Mahavajradhara	Hymn of 108 NameH of Maha vajraDara
   atha bhagavantaḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ punarapi samājamāgamyāsya	aTa BagavantaH sarva taTAgatAH punar api samAjam Agamya asya
   vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalasyādhiṣṭhānāyāśeṣānavaśeṣasya ca sattvadhātoḥ	vajra DAtu mahA maNxalasya aDizWAnAya aSeza an avaSezasya ca sattva DAtoH
   paritrāṇasarvahitasukhāvāptyai	paritrANa sarva hita suKa avAptyE
   yāvatsarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhijñābhisaṃbodhyuttamasiddhaye bhagavantaṃ	yAvat sarva taTAgata samatA jQAna aBijQA aBisaMboDi uttama sidDaye Bagavantam
   sarvatathāgatādhipatiṃ svavajrasattvamanādinidhanaṃ mahāvajradharamanena	sarva taTAgata aDipatim sva vajra sattvam anAdiniDanam mahA vajra Daram anena
   nāmāṣṭaśatenādhyeṣitavantaḥ //	nAma azwaSatena aDyezitavantaH //
   vajrasattvamahāsattva vajrasarvatathāgata /	vajra sattva mahA sattva vajra sarva taTAgataH /
   samantabhadra vajrādya vajrapāṇe namo 'stu te // 1 //	samantaBadra vajra adya vajrapANe namaH astu te // 1 //
   vajrarāja subuddhāgrya vajrāṅkuśatathāgata /	vajra rAja su budDa agrya vajrAFkuSa taTAgataH /
   amogharāja vajrāgrya vajrākarṣa namostu te // 2 //	amoGa rAja vajra agrya vajrAkarza namoH tu te // 2 //
   vajrarāga mahāsaukhya vajravāṇa vaśaṅkara /	vajra rAga mahA sOKya vajravANa vaSaFkara /
   bhārakāma mahāvajra vajracāpo namo 'stu te // 3 //	BAra kAma mahA vajra vajra cApaH namaH astu te // 3 //
   vajrasādho susattvāgrya vajratuṣṭi mahārate /	vajra sADo su sattva agrya vajra tuzwi mahArate /
   prāmodyarāja vajrāgraya vajraharṣa namo 'stu te // 4 //	prAmodya rAja vajra agraya vajra harza namaH astu te // 4 //
   vajraratna suvajrārthaṃ vajrākāśa mahāmaṇe /	vajra ratna su vajra arTam vajra AkASa mahA maNe /
   ākāśagarbha vajrāḍhya vajragarbha namostu te // 5 //	AkASa garBa vajra AXya vajragarBa namoH tu te // 5 //
   vajrateja mahājvāla vajrasūrya jinaprabha /	vajra teja mahA jvAla vajra sUrya jina praBaH /
   vajraraśmi mahāteja vajraprabha namo 'stu te // 6 //	vajra raSmi mahA teja vajrapraBa namaH astu te // 6 //
   vajraketu susattvārtha vajradhvaja sutoṣaka /	vajraketu su sattva arTa vajraDvaja sutozaka /
   ratnaketu mahāvajra vajrayaṣṭe namo 'stu te // 7 //	ratnaketu mahA vajra vajra yazwe namaH astu te // 7 //
   vajrahāsa mahāhāsa vajrasmita mahādbhuta /	vajrahAsa mahA hAsa vajra smita mahA adButa /
   prītiprāmodya vajrāgrya vajraprīte namo 'stu te // 8 //	prIti prAmodya vajra agrya vajra prIte namaH astu te // 8 //
   vajradharma sutatvārtha vajrapadma suśodhaka /	vajra Darma sutatva arTa vajra padma su SoDakaH /
   lokeśvara suvajrākṣa vajranetra namo 'stu te // 9 //	lokeSvara su vajrAkza vajra netra namaH astu te // 9 //

   "samayastvam" iti prokte pṛṣṭhataścandramāviśet /	"samayaH tvam" iti prokte pRzWatas candram AviSet /
   tatrātmā bhāvayetsatvaṃ "samayastvam" ahaṃ brūvan // 1 //	tatra AtmA BAvayet satvam "samayaH tvam" aham brUvan // 1 //
   yasya sattvasya yā mudrā tāmātmānantu bhāvayet /	yasya sattvasya yA mudrA tAm Atma Anantu BAvayet /
   sādhayedvajrajāpena sarvamudrāprasādhanam // 2 //	sADayet vajra jApena sarva mudrA prasADanam // 2 //
   "jaḥ hūṃ vaṃ hoḥ" bruvan kāye sarvabuddhān praveśayet /	"jaH hUm vam hoH" bruvan kAye sarva budDAn praveSayet /
   manasā sādhuyogena sādhanaṃ tvaparam mahad // iti // 3 //	manasA sADu yogena sADanam tu aparam mahat // iti // 3 //
   athāsāṃ karma pravakṣyāmi vajrakarma niruttaram /	aTa AsAm karma pravakzyAmi vajra karma niruttaram /
   buddhānusmṛtisaṃsiddhaḥ śīghraṃ buddhatvamāpnuyāt // 4 //	budDa anusmRti saMsidDaH SIGram budDa tvam ApnuyAt // 4 //
   sattvavajyā tu saṃsiddhaḥ sarvamudrādhipo bhavet /	sattva vajyA tu saMsidDaH sarva mudrA aDipaH Bavet /
   sattvavajra yāntu mudrāyāṃ sarvaratnādhipaḥ sa tu // 5 //	sattva vajra yAntu mudrAyAm sarva ratna aDipaH sa tu // 5 //
   siddhastu dharmavajra yā vai buddhadharmadharo bhavet /	sidDaH tu Darma vajra yA vE budDa Darma DaraH Bavet /
   karmavajriṇi mudrāyāṃ vajrakarmakaro bhavet // 6 //	karma vajriNi mudrAyAm vajra karma karaH Bavet // 6 //
   siddhyate vajrasattvastu bandhayā sattvamudrayā /	sidDyate vajra sattvaH tu banDayA sattva mudrayA /
   ākarṣayedvajradharāṃ vajrākarṣaprayogataḥ // 7 //	Akarzayet vajraDarAm vajra Akarza prayogataH // 7 //
   vajrarāgamahāmudrā sarvabuddhāṃstu rāgayet /	vajra rAga mahAmudrA sarva budDAn= tu rAgayet /
   toṣayetsarvabuddhānāṃ vajrasādhaprayogataḥ // 8 //	tozayet sarva budDAnAm vajra sADa prayogataH // 8 //
   dadyād buddhābhiṣekāṇi ratnamudrāvidhistathā /	dadyAt budDa aBizekANi ratnamudrA viDiH taTA /
   vajratejā bhavecchīghraṃ vajratejaḥprayogataḥ // 9 //	vajra tejAH Bavet SIGram vajra tejaH prayogataH // 9 //
   vajraketudharaṃ sevya bhavedāśāprapūrakaḥ /	vajraketu Daram sevya Bavet ASA prapUrakaH /
   vajrahāsavidhiṃ yojya sarvabuddhaiḥ samaṃ haset // 10 //	vajrahAsa viDim yojya sarva budDEH samam haset // 10 //
   vajradharmadharo bhūyād vajradharmaprayogataḥ /	vajra Darma DaraH BUyAt vajra Darma prayogataH /
   prajñāgryaḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ vajratīkṣṇaprayogataḥ // 11 //	prajQA agryaH sarva budDAnAm vajra tIkzNa prayogataH // 11 //
   vajracakradharaṃ sevya dharmacakraṃ sa vartayet /	vajra cakra Daram sevya Darma cakram sa vartayet /
   buddhavāksiddhimāpnoti vajrabhāṣaprayogataḥ // 12 //	budDa vAc sidDim Apnoti vajra BAza prayogataH // 12 //
   vajrakarma[gataṃ] kṣipraṃ vajrakarmāgryasādhanāt /	vajra karma[ gataM] kzipram vajra karma agrya sADanAt /
   nibadhya vajrakavacaṃ vajrakāyatvamāpnuyāt // 13 //	nibaDya vajra kavacam vajra kAya tvam ApnuyAt // 13 //
   vajrayakṣaṃ tu vai sādhya vajrayakṣasamo bhavet /	vajrayakzam tu vE sADya vajrayakza samaH Bavet /
   sarvamudrāprasiddhastu vajramuṣṭinibandhanān // 14 //	sarva mudrA prasidDaH tu vajra muzwi nibanDanAn // 14 //
   vajralāsyāṃ tu vai sādhya mahāvajraratiṃ labhet /	vajralAsyAm tu vE sADya mahA vajra ratim laBet /
   vajramālā nibandhastu sarvabuddhābhiṣekadaḥ // 15 //	vajramAlAH nibanDaH tu sarva budDa aBizeka daH // 15 //
   yojayedvajragītāṃ tu vajragītāprayogataḥ /	yojayet vajra gItAm tu vajra gIta aprayogataH /
   vajranṛtyāṃ tu saṃyojya sarvabuddhaiḥ sa pūjyate // 16 //	vajranRtyAm tu saMyojya sarva budDEH sa pUjyate // 16 //
   pralhādayejjagatsarvaṃ vajradhūpāprayogataḥ /	pralhAdayet jagat sarvam vajra DUpa aprayogataH /
   vajrapuṣpāṃ tu saṃyojya vaśīkuryājjagat sa tu // 17 //	vajrapuzpAm tu saMyojya vaSIkuryAt jagat sa tu // 17 //
   vajrālokamahāmudrā cakṣurdadyātprapūjayan /	vajra Aloka mahAmudrA cakzuH dadyAt prapUjayan /
   sarvaduḥkhaharo bhūyādvajragandhaprayogataḥ // 18 //	sarva duHKa haraH BUyAt vajra ganDa prayogataH // 18 //
   vajrāṅkuśasamākarṣāt sarvākarṣakaraḥ paraḥ /	vajra aFkuSa samAkarzAt sarva Akarza karaH paraH /
   sarvapraveśako bhūyād vajrapāśaprayogataḥ // 19 //	sarva praveSakaH BUyAt vajra pASa prayogataH // 19 //
   vajrasphoṭantu saṃyojya sarvabandhakṣayo bhaved /	vajra sPowantu saMyojya sarva banDa kzayaH Bavet /
   vajrāveśavidhiṃ yojya sarvāveśaprasādhaka // 20 // iti //	vajra AveSa viDim yojya sarva AveSa prasADakaH // 20 // iti //
   atha sarvatathāgatavajrasamayamudrājñānaṃ bhavati /	aTa sarva taTAgata vajra samaya mudrA jQAnam Bavati /
   añjaliṃ tu dṛḍhaṃ badhvā sarvāṅagulinibandhitam /	aQjalim tu dRXam baDvA sarvAFa guli nibanDitam /
   vajrāñjaliḥ samākhyāto vajrabandhaḥ subandha[nāt // 1 //	vajrAQjaliH samAKyAtaH vajrabanDaH subanDa[nAt // 1 //
   sarva] samayamudrāstu vajrabandhasamudbhavāḥ /	sarva] samaya mudrAH tu vajra banDa samudBavAH /
   tāsāṃ bandhaṃ pravakṣyāmi vajrabandhamanuttaram // 2 //	tAsAm banDam pravakzyAmi vajra banDam anuttaram // 2 //
   sattvavajrāṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya madhyamotthāsamāṅakurām /	sattva vajrAm dRXIkRtya maDyama utTa asamAFa kurAm /
   madhyamāntarasaṃkocān dvitīyā buddhavarṇitā // 3 //	maDyama antara saMkocAn dvitIyA budDa varNitA // 3 //
   madhyamāṅaguṣṭharatnā tu padmasaṃkocamadhyamā /	maDyamAFa guzWa ratnA tu padma saMkoca maDyamA /
   pañcamī buddhamudrā tu tathaivāgrasukuñcitā // 4 //	paQcamI budDamudrA tu taTA eva agra su kuQcitAH // 4 //
   athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi tathāgatakulasya hi /	aTa atas saMpravakzyAmi taTAgata kulasya hi /
   samayagrāhikā mudrā bandhaṃ siddhiṃ ca karma ca // 5 //	samaya grAhikAH mudrA banDam sidDim ca karma ca // 5 //
   pāṇidvayamaye candre madhyamāṅgulivarjite /	pANi dvaya maye candre maDyama aFguli varjite /
   antyāṅgulimukhāsaṅgāda vajraṃ vai sattvavajrayā // 6 //	antya aFguli muKa AsaFgAda vajram vE sattva vajrayA // 6 //
   agrāṅkuśāgrasaṃyogād sādhukārapradāyikā /	agra aFkuSa agra saMyogAt sADu kAra pradAyikA /
   vajrasatvacatuṣkasya siddhimudrāgaṇo hyayam // 7 //	vajra satva catuzkasya sidDi mudrA gaNaH hi ayam // 7 //
   ratnavajrā samāṅaguṣṭhatarjanīmukhasandhanāt /	ratna vajrA samAFa guzWa tarjanI muKa sanDanAt /
   sā eva madhyamānāmakaniṣṭhā suprasāritā // 8 //	sA eva maDyamA na Am akanizWA su prasAritAH // 8 //
   patākā tu samānāmakaniṣṭhābhyāṃ samanvitā /	patAkA tu samAna AmakanizWAByAm samanvitA /
   hāsasthānasthitā caiva sā eva parivartitā // 9 //	hAsa sTAna sTitA ca eva sA eva parivartitAH // 9 //
   prasāritasamāṅaguṣṭhasthitā kuñcitatarjanī /	prasArita samAFa guzWa sTitA kuQcita tarjanI /
   sā eva varjakośā tu madhyamā mukhasandhitā // 10 //	sA eva varjakoSA tu maDyamA muKa sanDi tA // 10 //
   sā eva tu samānāmakaniṣṭhā cakrasaṃjñitā /	sA eva tu samAna AmakanizWA cakra saMjQitAH /
   niryuktāṅaguṣṭhabandhā tu prasāritamukhotthitā // 11 //	niryukta aFa guzWa banDA tu prasArita muKa utTitAH // 11 //
   kaniṣṭhāṅaguṣṭhamukhayoḥ samājāt karmavarjitā /	kanizWAFa guzWa muKayoH samAjAt karma varjitA /
   sā eva tu samāgryā vai hṛdisthā suprasāritā // 12 //	sA eva tu samA agryA vE hRdisTA su prasAritAH // 12 //
   kuñcitāgr yāgradaṃṣṭrā tu kaniṣṭhā sandhimokṣitā /	kuQcita agr yAgra daMzwrA tu kanizWA sanDi mokzitA /
   kaniṣṭhāntarato 'ṅaguṣṭhau pīḍayetkuñcitāgryayā // 13 //	kanizWA antarataH aFaguzWO pIxayet kuQcita agryayA // 13 //
   hṛdaye tu samāṅaguṣṭhā suprasāritamālinī /	hRdaye tu samAFa guzWA su prasArita mAlinI /
   aṅagulyagramakhoddhāntā nṛtyato mūrdhni saṃyutā // 14 //	aFagulI agra maKa udDAntA nRtyataH mUrDni saMyutAH // 14 //
   vajrabandha tvadho dānāt svāñjaliścordhvadāyikā /	vajrabanDa tu aDas dAnAt sva aQjaliH ca UrDva dAyikAH /
   samāṅaguṣṭhanipīḍā ca suprasāritalepanā // 15 //	samAFa guzWa nipIxA ca su prasArita lepanA // 15 //
   ekatarjanīsaṃkocā dvyaṅaguṣṭhagranthibandhitā /	eka tarjanI saMkocAH dvi aFa guzWa granTi banDitA /
   aṅaguṣṭhāgra yakaṭā bandhā vajraṭamuṣṭyagrasandhitā // iti // 16 //	aFaguzWa agra yakawAH banDAH vajrawa muzwi agra sanDitA // iti // 16 //
   athāsāṃ sādhanaṃ vakṣye vajrasādhanamuttamam /	aTa AsAm sADanam vakzye vajra sADanam uttamam /
   svamudrayā hṛdisthayā sattvavajrasamādhinā // 17 //	sva mudrayA hRdisTayA sattva vajra samADinA // 17 //
   athāsāṃ karma vakṣyāmi vajrakarma niruttaram /	aTa AsAm karma vakzyAmi vajra karma niruttaram /
   vajradhātvādimudrāsu samājena tathāgatāḥ // 18 //	vajra DAtu Adi mudrAsu samAjena taTAgatAH // 18 //
   maṇḍalācāryaśiṣyāṇāmadhiṣṭhāsyanti tatkṣaṇāt /	maNxala AcArya SizyANAm aDizWAsyanti tad kzaNAt /
   sattvavajr yāntu baddhāyāṃ bhavedvajradharopamaḥ // 19 //	sattva vajr yAntu badDAyAm Bavet vajraDara upamaH // 19 //
   vajrāṅkuśyāṃ baddhamātrāyāṃ sarvabuddhāṃ samāh vayet /	vajrAFkuSyAm badDa mAtrAyAm sarva budDAm samAm vayet /
   rāgavajraprayogeṇa sa buddhānapi rāgayet // 20 //	rAga vajra prayogeNa sa budDAn api rAgayet // 20 //
   [vajrasādhubandhena buddhadānatuṣṭiṃ labhati /]	[vajra sADu banDena budDa dAna tuzwim laBati /]
   vajratuṣṭyā jinaiḥ sarvaiḥ sādhukāraiḥ praśaṃsyate // 21 //	vajra tuzwyA jinEH sarvEH sADukArEH praSaMsyate // 21 //
   ratnavajr yāntu baddhāyāṃ buddhaiḥ so 'pyabhiṣicyate /	ratna vajr yAntu badDAyAm budDEH saH api aBizicyate /
   vajrasūryāṃ badhvā vai bhaved buddhaprabhopamaḥ // 22 //	vajra sUryAm baDvA vE Bavet budDa praBA upamaH // 22 //
   vajraketudharo bhūtvā sarvāśāḥ sa tu pūrayet /	vajraketu DaraH BUtvA sarva ASAH sa tu pUrayet /
   vajrahāsaprayogeṇa sarvabuddhaiḥ samaṃ haset // 23 //	vajrahAsa prayogeNa sarva budDEH samam haset // 23 //
   dharmavajrāṃ samādhāya vajradharmopamo bhavet /	Darma vajrAm samADAya vajra Darma upamaH Bavet /
   vajrakośāṃ tu saṃgṛhya sarvakleśāṃ cchinatti saḥ // 24 //	vajra koSAm tu saMgRhya sarva kleSAm cCinatti saH // 24 //
   vajracakrāṃ dṛḍhīkṛtvā maṇḍalādhipatirbhavet /	vajra cakrAm dRXIkRtvA maNxala aDipatiH Bavet /
   vajrabhāṣaprayogeṇa vajravāksiddhiruttamā // 25 //	vajra BAza prayogeNa vajra vAc sidDiH uttamAH // 25 //
   karmavajrāṃ tu sandhāya vajrakarmasamo bhavet /	karma vajrAm tu sanDAya vajra karma samaH Bavet /
   vajravarmāṃ dṛḍhīkṛtvā kāyo vajramayo bhavet // 26 //	vajravarmAm dRXIkRtvA kAyaH vajra mayaH Bavet // 26 //
   vajradaṃṣṭrāgramudrayā duṣṭamārāṃ sa bhañjati /	vajra daMzwra agra mudrayA duzwam ArAm sa BaQjati /
   vajramuṣṭiṃ dṛḍhāṃ badhvā sarvamudrāṃ vaśannayet // 27 //	vajra muzwim dRXAm baDvA sarva mudrAm vaSan nayet // 27 //
   lāsyayā ratayo divyāḥ mālayā bhūṣaṇāni ca /	lAsyayA ratayaH divyAH mAlayA BUzaNAni ca /
   gītayā sphuṭavāco nityaṃ pūjāṃ labhati nṛtyayā // 28 //	gItayA sPuwa vAcaH nityam pUjAm laBati nRtyayA // 28 //
   dhūpayā lhādayed loka puṣpayā rūpaśobhitām /	DUpayA lhAdayet loka puzpayA rUpa SoBitAm /
   dīpayā lokaśuddhitvaṃ gandhayā divyagandhatām // 29 //	dIpayA loka SudDi tvam ganDayA divya ganDa tAm // 29 //
   vajrāṅakuśaḥ samākarṣed vajrapāśā praveśayet /	vajrAFa kuSaH samAkarzet vajra pASA praveSayet /
   vajrasphoṭā tu bandhayād vajraghaṇṭā samāviśed // 30 // iti //	vajrasPowA tu banDayAt vajra GaNwA samAviSet // 30 // iti //
   atha dhamamudrā bhavanti /	aTa Dama mudrAH Bavanti /
   vajrajñānaṃ tu buddhānāṃ vajradhātu dṛḍhaṃkaram /	vajra jQAnam tu budDAnAm vajraDAtu dRXaMkaram /
   ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmamudrā yathāvidhi // 1 //	atas param pravakzyAmi DarmamudrA yaTAviDi // 1 //
   "samayastvam" iti prokte sarvamudrāpatirbhavet /	"samayaH tvam" iti prokte sarva mudrA patiH Bavet /
   "anyasva" iti vai prokte buddhānākarṣayed dhruvam // 2 //	"anya sva" iti vE prokte budDAn Akarzayet Druvam // 2 //
   "aho sukha" iti prokte buddhānapi sa rāgayet /	"aho suKa" iti prokte budDAn api sa rAgayet /
   "sādhu sādhv" iti vai proktvā sādhukāraiḥ sa toṣayet // 3 //	"sADu sADv" iti vE proktvA sADukArEH sa tozayet // 3 //
   "sumaha[ttvam" iti] prokte sarvabuddhābhiṣecanam /	"su maha[ttvam" iti] prokte sarva budDa aBizecanam /
   "rūpodyote"  ti vai prokte dharmatejo bhaviṣyati // 4 //	"rUpa udyote" ti vE prokte Darma tejaH Bavizyati // 4 //
   "arthaprāptira" iti prokte sarvāśāḥ pūrayet sa tu /	"arTa prAptiH a" iti prokte sarva ASAH pUrayet sa tu /
   "ha ha hūṃ he  "[ti prokte samabuddhahāsaṃ prāpnu] yāt // 5 //	"ha ha hUm he "[ti prokte sama budDa hAsam prApnu] yAt // 5 //
   "sarvakāri" iti prokte akāryamapi śodhayet /	"sarva kAri" iti prokte akAryam api SoDayet /
   "duḥ khaccheda" iti prokte sarvaduḥkhāñchinatti saḥ // 6 //	"duH KacCeda" iti prokte sarva duHKAQCinatti saH // 6 //
   ["buddha bodhi" iti] prokte maṇḍalādhipatirbhavet /	["budDa boDi" iti] prokte maNxala aDipatiH Bavet /
   "pratiśabda" iti prokte buddhaiḥ sahasamālapet // 7 ///	"pratiSabda" iti prokte budDEH saha samAlapet // 7 ///
   "śubhasiddham" iti prokte vaśitvaṃ sarvato bhavet /	"SuBa sidDam" iti prokte vaSitvam sarvatas Bavet /
   ["nirbhayastvam" iti] prokte nirbhayo bhavettatkṣaṇāt // 8 //	["nirBayaH tvam" iti] prokte nirBayaH Bavet tad kzaNAt // 8 //
   "śatru bhakṣa" iti prokte sarvaśatrun sa bhakṣayet /	"Satru Bakza" iti prokte sarva Satrun sa Bakzayet /
   "sarvasiddhir" iti prokte sarvasiddhirbhaviṣyati // 9 //	"sarva sidDir" iti prokte sarva sidDiH Bavizyati // 9 //
   ["mahārati" ratiṃ] divyāṃ "rūpaśobhā" tathaiva ca /	[" mahArati" ratiM] divyAm "rUpa SoBA" taTA eva ca /
   "śrotrasaukhyā" sukhaṃ dadyāt "sarvapūjā" supūjatām // 10 //	"Srotra sOKyA" suKam dadyAt "sarva pUjA" su pUjatAm // 10 //
   "pralhādini" manaḥsaukhyaṃ "phalāgamī" phalāgamā /	"pralhAdini" manaH sOKyam "Pala AgamI" Pala AgamA /
   "su[tejāgri" mahātejaḥ] "sugandhāṅgi" sugandhatām // 11 //	"su[teja agri" mahA tejaH] "suganDAFgi" suganDa tAm // 11 //
   "ayāhi jaḥ" samākarṣā "ahi hūṃ hūṃ" praveśikā /	"ayAhi jaH" samAkarzA "ahi hUm hUM" praveSikAH /
   "hesphoṭa vaṃ" mahābandhā "ghaṇṭā aḥ aḥ" pracālite  // ti // 12 //	"hesPowa vaM" mahAbanDAH "GaNwAH aH aH" pracAlite // ti // 12 //
   athāsāṃ dharmamudrā [sādhanaṃ pra] vakṣyate śubham /	aTa AsAm DarmamudrA [sADanam pra] vakzyate SuBam /
   jivhāyāṃ bhāvayed vajrāṃ sarvakarmāṇi kurvate // ti // 13 //	jivhAyAm BAvayet vajrAm sarva karmANi kurvate // ti // 13 //
   atha karmamudrābandho bhavati /	aTa karma mudrA banDaH Bavati /
   vajramuṣṭiṃ dṛḍhāṃ badhvā dvidhīkuryātsamāhitaḥ /	vajra muzwim dRXAm baDvA dviDIkuryAt samAhitaH /
   vajramudrādvayaṃ bhūyāt tato bandhaḥ pravakṣyate // 1 //	vajra mudrA dvayam BUyAt tatas banDaH pravakzyate // 1 //
   vāmavajrāṅagulirgrāhyaṃ dakṣiṇena samutthitā /	vAma vajrAFa guliH grAhyam dakziNena samutTitA /
   bodhāgrī nāma mudreyaṃ buddhabodhipradāyikā // 2 //	boDAgrI nAma mudrA iyam budDa boDi pradAyikA // 2 //
   akṣobhyasya bhūmisparśā ratne tu varadā tathā /	akzoByasya BUmi sparSA ratne tu vara dA taTA /
   amitāyoḥ samādhyagrā amoghasyābhayapradā // 3 //	amitAyoH samADi agrA amoGasya aBaya pradA // 3 //
   ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi karmamudrā samāsataḥ /	atas param pravakzyAmi karma mudrA samAsatas /
   vajrasattvādisattvānāṃ vajrakarmapravartikāḥ // 4 //	vajra sattva Adi sattvAnAm vajra karma pravartikAH // 4 //
   sagarvotkarṣaṇaṃ dvābhyāmaṅku śagrahasaṃsthitā /	sa garva utkarzaNam dvAByAm aFku Sagraha saMsTitA /
   vāṇaghantanayogācca sādhukārā hṛdi sthitā // 5 //	vANa Gantana yogAt ca sADu kArA hRdi sTitAH // 5 //
   abhiṣeke dvivajraṃ tu hṛdi sūryapradarśanam /	aBizeke dvi vajram tu hRdi sUrya pradarSanam /
   vāmasthabāhudaṇḍā ca tathāsye parivartitā // 6 //	vAma sTa bAhu daNxA ca taTA Asye parivartitAH // 6 //

   Mudra	Mudra
   tato vajrakuladharmarahasyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet /	tatas vajra kula Darma rahasya mudrA jQAnam Sikzayet /

   phaṭ //	Paw //

   Emanation of deities from samadhi	Emanation of deitieH from samaDi

   hūṃ //	hUm //

   CHAPTER 16 PADMA GUHYA MUDRA MANDALA VIDHI VISTARA	CHA aPTER 16 PADMA GUHYa a MUDRa a MANDALA  VIDHI VISTARA
   Emanation of deities from samadhi	Emanation of deitieH from samaDi
   atha bhagavān punarapi	aTa BagavAn punar api
   sarvatathāgatadharmadhāraṇīsamayasaṃbhavamudrādhiṣṭhānapadmannāma samādhiṃ	sarva taTAgata Darma DAraNI samaya saMBava mudrA aDizWAna padmat nAma samADim
   samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamāmabhāṣat oṃ sarvatathāgatadharmasamaye hūṃ //	samApadya imAm sva vidyA uttamAm aBAzat om sarva taTAgata Darma samaye hUm //
   atha vajrapāṇirmahābodhisatvaḥ imāṃ svakulasaṃbhavāṃ vidyottamāmabhāṣat oṃ	aTa vajrapANiH mahAboDisatvaH imAm sva kula saMBavAm vidyA uttamAm aBAzat om
   vajrasamaye hūṃ //	vajra samaye hUm //
   atha vajragarbho bodhisatva mahāsatva imāṃ svavidyottamāmabhāṣat oṃ	aTa vajragarBaH boDisatva mahAsatvaH imAm sva vidyA uttamAm aBAzat om
   maṇiratnasamaye hūṃ //	maNi ratna samaye hUm //
   atha vajranetro bodhisatva imāṃ svavidyottamāmabhāṣat oṃ padmasamaye hūṃ	aTa vajra netraH boDisatvaH imAm sva vidyA uttamAm aBAzat om padma samaye hUm
   atha vajraviśvo bodhisatva imāṃ svavidyottamāmabhāṣat oṃ karmasamaye hūṃ	aTa vajra viSvaH boDisatvaH imAm sva vidyA uttamAm aBAzat om karma samaye hUm
   atha bhagavānāryāvalokiteśvaro bodhisatva idaṃ	aTa BagavAn Arya avalokita ISvaraH boDisatvaH idam

   atha vajrapāṇirmahābrodhisatva idaṃ	aTa vajrapANiH mahA broDisatvaH idam

   buddhabimbānadhiṣṭhāya svahṛdistu praveśayet // 1 //	budDa bimbAn aDizWAya sva hRdiH tu praveSayet // 1 //

   atha samayamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati /	aTa samayamudrA uttama sidDi tantram Bavati /

   atha dharmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati /	aTa DarmamudrA uttama sidDi tantram Bavati /

   yathā vajradharaḥ siddhistathāhamiti bhāvayan /	yaTA vajraDaraH sidDiH taTA aham iti BAvayan /
   mahāmudrāprayogeṇa kṣaṇātsauritvamāpnuta // iti //	mahAmudrA prayogeNa kzaNAt sOri tvam Apnuta // iti //
   atha dharmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati /	aTa DarmamudrA uttama sidDi tantram Bavati /
   anakṣareṣu dharmeṣu prapañco na hi vidyate /	anakzarezu Darmezu prapaQcaH na hi vidyate /

   mahāmudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati /	mahAmudrA uttama sidDi tantram Bavati /
   sarvabuddhābhiṣeko 'haṃ bhaveyaṃ vajragarbhavat /	sarva budDa aBizekaH aham Baveyam vajra garBa vat /

   sarvakulamudrāṇāṃ buddhabodhisatvottamasiddhyavāptividhivistaraḥ //	sarva kula mudrANAm budDa boDisatva uttama sidDi avApti viDi vistaraH //
   atha vajrapāṇirmahābodhisatvaḥ punarapi	aTa vajrapANiH mahA boDisatvaH punar api

   sarvakulasamayavidhivistaratantraṃ //	sarva kula samaya viDi vistara tantram //
   atha vajrapāṇirmahābodhisatvaḥ	aTa vajrapANiH mahAboDisatvaH
   sarvatathāgatadharmamudrājñānasiddhitantramudājahāra / tatreyaṃ	sarva taTAgata Darma mudrA jQAna sidDi tantram udAjahAraH / tatra iyam
   sarvatathāgatadharmasiddhitantra bhavati /	sarva taTAgata Darma sidDi tantra Bavati /
   buddho dharma iti khyāta ityuktvā dharmatākṣaraṃ /	budDaH DarmaH iti KyAtaH iti uktvA DarmatA akzaram /
   buddhadharmamahāmudrājñānasya paramanayaṃ //	budDa Darma mahAmudrA jQAnasya param anayam //
   tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmasiddhitantraṃ /	tatra idam taTAgata kula Darma sidDi tantram /

   aliptaṃ salilaiḥ padmaṃ tathā rāgo na duṣyati /	aliptam salilEH padmam taTA rAgaH na duzyati /
   iti brūvannakāryāṇi kurvaṃ pāpairna lipyate //	iti brUvanna kAryANi kurvam pApEH na lipyate //

   sarvakulakarmasiddhividhivistaratantraṃ //	sarva kula karma sidDi viDi vistara tantram //

   tatredaṃ vajrakulasamādhisiddhitantraṃ /	tatra idam vajra kula samADi sidDi tantram /

   CHAPTER 24 SARVA KULA KALPA GUHYA VIDHI VISTARA TANTRA	CHA aPTER 24 SARVA  KULa a  KALPa a GUHYA  VIDHI VI STARA a TANTRA

   CHAPTER 25 SARVA KALPA GUHYOTTARA TANTRA VIDHI VISTARA	CHA aPTER 25 SARVA  Ka ALPa a GUHYOTTAH Ra a TANTRA  VIDHI VISTARA
   atha vajrapāṇirmahābodhisatvaḥ	aTa vajrapANiH mahAboDisatvaH
   sarvatathāgatadharmottamasiddhitantramudājahāra / tatredaṃ	sarva taTAgata Darma uttama sidDi tantram udAjahAraH / tatra idam
   tathāgatadharmottamasiddhitantraṃ	taTAgata Darma uttama sidDi tantram
   buddhadharmasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /	budDa Darma samADim tu BAvayan su samAhitaH /
   buddhānusmṛtiyogena siddhimāpnotyuttamām //	budDa anusmRti yogena sidDim Apnoti uttamAm //
   ityāha bhagavāṃstathāgataḥ /	iti Aha BagavAn= taTAgataH /
   tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmottamasiddhitantraṃ /	tatra idam taTAgata kula Darma uttama sidDi tantram /

   ityāha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamādhiḥ //	iti Aha BagavAn sarva taTAgata samADiH //
   tatredaṃ vajrakuladharmottamasiddhitantraṃ /	tatra idam vajra kula Darma uttama sidDi tantram /
   trilokavijayākāraṃ bhāvayan puratastathā /	triloka vijaya AkAram BAvayan puratas taTA /
   vajrapāṇibalo bhūtvā trilokavijayī bhaved //	vajrapANi balaH BUtvA triloka vijayI Bavet //
   ityāha bhagavān vajrasatvaḥ //	iti Aha BagavAn vajra satvaH //
   tatredaṃ padmakuladharmottamasiddhitantraṃ /	tatra idam padma kula Darma uttama sidDi tantram /
   jagadvinayadharmaṃ tu bhāvayan puratasta[thā /]	jagat vinaya Darmam tu BAvayan puratas ta[TAH /]
   sarvākāravaropetaṃ vinayaṃ prakaroti sa //	sarva AkAra vara upetam vinayam prakaroti saH //
   ityāha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ //	iti Aha BagavAn vajra DarmaH //
   tatredaṃ maṇikuladharmottamasiddhitantraṃ /	tatra idam maNi kula Darma uttama sidDi tantram /
   sarvārthasiddhirā[kāraṃ bhāvayan puratastathā /	sarva arTa sidDiH A[kAram BAvayan puratas taTA /

   sarvakuladharmottamasiddhividhivistaratantraṃ //	sarva kula Darma uttama sidDi viDi vistara tantram //

   sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa buddhasiddhimavāpnute  //	sUkzma vajra prayogeNa budDa sidDim avApnute //

   tyāha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ /	tyAha BagavAn vajra DarmaH /

   vajratīkṣṇa mahākośa prajñājñāna mahāmate /	vajra tIkzNa mahA koSa prajQA jQAna mahAmate /
   pāpaccheda ma[hākhaḍga bu]ddhaśastra namo 'stu te // 10 //	pApa= Ceda ma[hA Kaxga bu]dDa Sastra namaH astu te // 10 //
   vajrahetu mahācakra buddhacakra mahānidhi /	vajra hetu mahAcakra budDacakra mahAniDi /
   sarvamaṇḍala dharmāgra dharmacakra namo 'stu te // 11 //	sarva maNxala Darma agra Darma cakra namaH astu te // 11 //
   vajrabhā[ṣa mahābhāṣa] niḥprapañca mahākṣara /	vajraBA[za mahABAza] niHprapaQca mahA kzara /
   anakṣara mahājāpa buddhavāca namo 'stu te // 12 //	anakzara mahA jApa budDa vAca namaH astu te // 12 //
   vajrakarma sukarmāgrya mahākarma sukarmakṛt /	vajra karma su karma agrya mahA karma su karma kRt /
   guhyapū[ja mahāpūja buddhapūja namo]stu te // 13 //	guhya pU[ja mahA pUja budDa pUja namo]H tu te // 13 //
   vajrarakṣa mahāvarma kavacāgrya mahādṛḍha /	vajrarakza mahA varma kavaca agrya mahA dRXaH /
   mahārakṣa mahāsāra buddhavīrya namo 'stu te // 14 //	mahArakza mahAsAra budDa vIrya namaH astu te // 14 //
   vajrayakṣa mahākrodha sarvaduṣṭabhayānaka /	vajrayakza mahA kroDa sarva duzwa BayAnakaH /
   sarvabuddhamahopāya agrayakṣa namo 'stu te // 15 //	sarva budDa mahA upAya agra yakza namaH astu te // 15 //
   mahāsandhi mahāmudra mahāsamayabandhaka /	mahAsanDi mahAmudra mahA samaya banDaka /
   mahāmuṣṭe samudrāgrya vajramuṣṭe namo 'stu te // 16 //	mahA muzwe samudra agrya vajra muzwe namaH astu te // 16 //
   vandyo mānyaśca pūjyaśca satkartavyastathāgataiḥ /	vandyaH mAnyaH ca pUjyaH ca satkartavyaH taTAgatEH /
   yasmādanādinidhanaṃ bodhicittaṃ tvamucyase // 17 //	yasmAt anAdiniDanam boDi cittam tvam ucyase // 17 //
   tvāmāsādya jināḥ sarve bodhisatvāśca śauriṇaḥ /	tvAm AsAdya jinAH sarve boDisatvAH ca SOriNaH /
   saṃbhūtā saṃbhaviṣyanti buddhabodhyagrahetavaḥ // 18 //	saMBUtA saMBavizyanti budDa boDi agra hetavaH // 18 //
   namaste vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya ca te namaḥ /	namaH te vajra sattvAya vajra ratnAya ca te namaH /
   namaste vajradharmāya namaste vajrakarmaṇe // 19 //	namaH te vajra DarmAya namaH te vajrakarmaNe // 19 //
   tvāmabhiṣṭutya nāmāgraiḥ praṇamya ca subhāvataḥ /	tvAm aBizwutya nAma agrEH praNamya ca suBAvataH /
   yatpuṇyaṃ tena sarvo hi buddhabodhimavāpnuyāt // 20 //	yat puNyam tena sarvaH hi budDa boDim avApnuyAt // 20 //
   yedamuccārayetsamyagnāmāṣṭaśatamuttamaṃ /	yA idam uccArayet samyak nAma azwaSatam uttamam /
   sakṛdvāraṃ subhaktisthaḥ sarvabuddhatvamāpnuyād //	sakRt vAram su Bakti sTaH sarva budDa tvam ApnuyAt //
   ityāha bhagavān buddhaḥ //	iti Aha BagavAn budDaH //
   atha vajrapāṇiṃ mahābodhisatvaṃ te sarvatathāgatā [ekakaṣṭhe]na	aTa vajrapANim mahA boDisatvam te sarva taTAgatAH [eka kazWe]na
   sādhukārāṇyanuprādān //	sADu kArANi anuprAdAn //
   sādhu te vajrasatvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /	sADu te vajra satvAya vajra ratnAya sADu te /
   vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe //	vajra DarmAya te sADu sADu te vajrakarmaNe //
   subhāṣitami[daṃ sūtraṃ] vajrayānamanuttaraṃ /	suBAzitam i[dam sUtraM] vajrayAnam anuttaram /
   sarvatathāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham //iti //	sarva taTAgatam guhyam mahA yAna aBisaMgraham //iti //
   idam [avocadbhagavānāttamanāḥ satathāratāryabodhisatvaśca sarvaḥ svahṛdaye	idam [avocat BagavAn AttamanAH sa taTAra tArya boDisatvaH ca sarvaH sva hRdaye
   praviśya bhagavataśca vajrasatvasya ca] bhāṣitamabhyanandanniti //	praviSya BagavataH ca vajra satvasya ca] BAzitam aByanandan= iti //
   [sarvatathāgatatatvasaṃgrahaṃ nāma mahāyānasū]traṃ samāptam //	[sarvataTAgatatatvasaMgraham nAma mahAyAna sU]tram samAptam //
